vidhAnagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLE mUlakAraNavembudannu I vyatyAsa
gaLa pariSIlaneyinda tiLiyabahudu.

## 3.3.1 tayArike mattu baLake
hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU mattu varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLigU
naDuve avugaLa tayArike mattu baLakegaLalli vyatyAsavide. hesarisuva
nAmapadagaLalli pratiyondannU bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli avugaLa
avaSyakate tOribandAga bhASeyannu baLasuva obba vyakti tayArisiru
tAne illavE bEre bhASeyinda eravalAgi paDediruttAne. anantara
samAjada mannaNe paDedu, intaha padagaLellavU ondondAgi
bhASeyalli baLakege bandiruttave. idakke viruddhavAgi, varNisuva
nAmapadagucchagaLu avannu baLasabEkAgiruva pratiyondu sandarbha
dallU vyAkaraNa niyamagaLiganusAravAgi punaH punaH racitavAguttave.

udAharaNegAgi ugibanDi emba hesarisuva nAmapadavannu pari
SIlisabahudu. adu hesarisuva sAdhana namma gamanakke illavE upa
yOgakke bandAga adannu hesarisuvudakkAgi yArO obbaru A
padavannu racisirabEku. mattu anantara itararU A pada sariyAdu
dendu adannu baLasatoDagidudarinda adu namma bhASeyalli baLakege
bandirabEku. idakke badalAgi, bassu emba pada sUcisuva intahadE
innondu sAdhanavannu nAvu baLasatoDagidAga adannu hesarisalu
ingliS bhASeyinda padavondannu eravalAgi paDediddu, A padavE
rUDige bandirabEku. intaha hesarisuva nAmapadagaLella ondalla ondu
sandarbhadalli tayArAgi illavE eravalAgi bEre bhASegaLinda bandu
namma bhASeyalli rUDhiyAgiruva padagaLu.

varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLa baLake I rItiyadalla. obba vyakti
illavE ondu vastuvannu gurutisabEkAdAga, avugaLalli kANisuva
illavE bEre rItiyalli namma gOcarakke baruva guNadharmagaLa
llondannu Arisi, adara mUlaka A vyakti illavE vastuvannu varNisi
hELalu nAmapadagucchavondannu racisikoLLuttEve.

udAharaNegAgi mEjina mEle mUru nAlku cenDugaLiddu
avallondannu gurutisi hELalu (endare itara cenDugaLinda adannu
pratyEkisi hELalu) A cenDinalli kANisuva mattu itara cenDugaLalli
kANisadiruva guNadharmavondannu ArisikoLLuttEve, mattu adannu
sUcisuvantaha padagucchavondannu racisikoLLuttEve. I rIti, sandarbha


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


kkanusAravAgi, kempu cenDu, doDDa cenDu, oDeda cenDu
modalAda padagucchagaLallondannu racisi, adu A guNadharmavannu
varNisuvudara mUlaka nAvu gurutisabEkAgiruva cenDannu gurutisu
vante mADuttEve.

## 3.3.2 guNadharmada Ayke
mEle sUcisiruva vyatyAsada phalavEnendare, hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu
sUcisuva guNadharma avannu baLasuva sandarbhadalli avu gurutisa
bEkAgiruva vastuvinalli iralEbEkendilla. Adare, varNisuva nAmapada
gucchagaLu sUcisuva guNadharma avannu baLasuva sandarbhagaLallella
avaSyavAgiyU avu gurutisabEkAgiruva vastuvinalli iralEbEkemba
niyamavide. hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu sUcisuva guNadharma A
hesarannu utpAdisuva samayadalli mAtravE avu gurutisuva vastu
vinalli iddiralu sAdhyavide.

udAharaNegAgi, hosamane emba nAmapada ondu vaThAradalli
iruva ondu manege A vaThAradavaru koTTiruva mattu anantara
rUDhige bandiruva hesarAgiralu sAdhyavide. A mane haLeyadAda
mElU adannu adE hesarininda gurutisuttiralu sAdhyavide, mattu
bEre halavAru hosa hosa manegaLannu adara sutta mutta
kaTTalAgideyAdarU, A haLeyadAgiruva maneyannE hosamaneyemba
hesarininda gurutisuttiralu sAdhyavide.

mEle koTTiruva karihalageyemba padada baLakeyU idE rIti
yadu. A padavannu modala bArige tayArisi, baLasida samayadalli
upAdhyAyaru klAsinalli bareyalu baLasuttidda sAdhana halagege kappu
baNNa baLiyuvudara mUlaka racitavAgiddudAgirabEku. hAgAgi,
karihalage emba hesaru Avattina kAladalli sariyAgiyE A sAdhanada
guNadharmavondannu sUcisuttittu. Adare, anantara bEre bEre baNNada
mattu bEre bEre dravyagaLinda mADida sAdhanagaLu A kAryakkAgi
baLakege bandiveyAdarU karihalage emba A sAdhanada hesaru
badalAgade hAgeyE rUDhiyalli uLidide.

illi gamanisabEkAda amSavEnendare, hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU
mattu varNisuva nAmapadagaLigU naDuve avu sUcisabEkAgiruva
guNadharmavannu AydukoLLuva kramadalli vyatyAsavide. hesarugaLu
sUcisuva guNadharma A padagaLannu tayArisuva samayadalli Ayke


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


goLLuttade, Adare varNanegaLu sUcisuva guNadharma avannu baLasuva
sandarbhagaLallella pratiyondu bAriyU punaH punaH AykegoLa
gAguttiruttade. I kAraNadindAgi, hesarannu baLasuva sandarbhagaLalli
varNanegaLannu baLasuvAga iruva hAge avu sUcisuva guNadharma
janara manassinalli iruvudilla.

udAharaNegAgi, karihalage emba padavannu prayOgisidAga, ondu
viSiSTavAda sAdhana namma manassige baruvudallade, 'kappu baNNa' illavE
'halageyinda racitavAda sAdhana' emba amSagaLu namma manassige
baruvudilla. kelavu viSiSTavAda sandarbhagaLalli mAtra ivu namma
gamanakke bandu, illavE yArAdarU ivannu namma gamanakke tandu,
antaha samayadalli A hesarigU mattu adu gurutisuva vastuvigU
naDuve guNadharmada maTTige asAngatyavideyemba viSaya namma
gamanakke baruttade.

guNadharmada Aykeyalli hesarugaLigU mattu varNanegaLigU
naDuve innondu vyatyAsavide. ondu vastuvannu hesarisuvAga, adaralli
kANisuva halavAru guNadharmagaLalli ondannu AydukoLLabEkAguttade.
udAharaNegAgi, jilijanaka embudu ondu viSiSTavAda anilada
hesaru. idu nIrina ondu ghaTakavAgiddu, Amlajanakavemba innondu
aniladoDane sEri nIrannunTumADuva guNadharma idakkide. I guNa
dharmada AdhArada mEle idannu jilijanaka emba hesarininda
kareyalAgide.

I ondu guNadharma mAtravallade bEreyU halakelavu guNa
dharmagaLu jalijanakavemba I anilakkive. udAharaNegAgi, idu
atyanta haguravAda, baNNavU vAsaneyU illada, kaNNige kANisada
ondu mUla dhAtu. idannu hesarisalu I guNadharmagaLalli yAvu
dannu bEkiddarU ArisikoLLabahudittu. Adare nIrina ghaTakavemba amSa
mukhyavAgi tOrida kAraNa, adannE A hesarannu tayArisuvavaru
ArisikonDirabEku. sAmAnyavAgi kaNNige athavA manassige eddu kANisu
vantaha mattu SASvatavAgi uLiyabahudendu manassige anisuvantaha
guNadharmavannu vastuvondakke hesariDuvAga ArisikoLLuvudu rUDhi.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa utpAdaneyalli kANisuva I Aykeyemba
amSa varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLa utpAdane illavE baLakeyalli
kANisuvudilla. ondu vastuvinalli eSTellA guNadharmagaLiveyO
avellavannU bEre bEre varNisuva padagucchagaLa mUlaka sUcisalu

sAdhyavide. I guNadharmagaLu SASvatavirabahudu, illavE kSaNikavira
bahudu; kaNNige eddu kANisuvantahavirabahudu, illavE aspaSTavAdu
vAgiralUbahudu.

idallade, hesarisuvudakkAgi guNadharmavondannu ArisuvAga,
hesarisabEkAgiruva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLannu antahavE itara
vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLiginta bhinnavAdavugaLembudannu tOrisa
ballantaha guNadharmavannE ArisikoLLuva krama rUDhiyallide. udA
haraNegAgi, yuddhadalli toDagiruva saynikaralli kAlinalli calisi
kAdADuvavarannu hesarisalu kAlALu emba pada rUDhige bandide. I
hesaru kudureya mEle illavE Aneya mEle kuLitu kAdADuva
itara saynikariginta avaru bhinnarAgiruvudannu sUcisuttade. bEre
sandarbha gaLalli kAlininda calisuvavarannu (udA: rasteyalli
calisuvavarannu) kAlALu emba I pada gurutisalAradu. avaru
saykal, skUTar, kAru modalAdavugaLalli calisuvavariginta bEre
embudannu sUcisalu pAdacAri emba samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda
bEreyE ondu hesaru rUDhige bandide.

## 3.3.3 arthadalli vyatyAsa
varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLige artha hELuvudu sulabha. avugaLa anga
gaLAgi bandiruva pada mattu pratyayagaLinda siddhavAguva arthavE
avugaLa arthavU Agiruvudarinda I kelasavannu bhASeyannu baLasu
vavarellarU mADaballaru. udAharaNegAgi kempu cenDu emba
varNisuva nAmapadagucchakke artha hELuvudu sulabha. kempu mattu
cenDu emba eraDu padagaLa sErikeyinda I padagucchavannu tayArisa
lAgiddu, 'kempAgiruva cenDu' embudAgi idakke arthavannu hELa
bahudu.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu ivakkinta tIra bhinnavAdavugaLu. mEle
sUcisidante, avugaLa arthavEnembudannu tiLiyalu A padagaLa oLa
racane sahAyakavAgaballudAdarU adondE avugaLa arthakke AdhAra
vAgalAradu. hesarisuva nAmapadavondu entaha vastugaLannu illavE
vyaktigaLannu hesarisuttade, mattu avugaLalli samAnavAgiruva guNadharma
gaLu yAvuvu embudannu pariSIlisida mElEnE A padakke sariyAda
arthavannu hELalu sAdhyavAdItu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


udAharaNegAgi hogesoppu emba nAmapadavannu pariSIlisa
bahudu. idondu hesarisuva nAmapada. hoge mattu soppu emba
eraDu padagaLa jODaNeyinda I pada tayArAgide. adara I
oLaracane adara arthavEnembudannu sUkSmavAgi tiLisaballudu, Adare
spaSTavAgi tiLisalAradu. ellA rItiya elegaLannu urisidAgalU hoge
horabaruttade. Adare avannella nAvu hogesoppu emba hesarininda
kareyuvudilla. hoge sEduvudakkAgi bIDi, sigarET modalAduvannu
tayArisalu baLasuva, mattu hogeyannu barisadEnE nEravAgi bAya
lliTTu jagiyuva, illavE puDimADi nasyavAgi baLasuva ondu viSiSTa
vAda giDavannu mattu adara eleyannu mAtravE adu gurutisuttade.
I giDada guNadharmagaLannu mAtravE hogesoppu emba padakke
artha hELuvAga baLasikoLLalu sAdhya.

mEle koTTiruva jalajanaka emba padada arthavU hIgeyE.
'nIrannunTumADuva anila' embudAgi bariya oLaracaneya AdhArada
mEle adakke artha koTTevAdare adu tappAdItu. yAkendare, Amla
janakavemba innondu anilavU (jalajanakada jate sEri) nIrannunTu
mADaballudu. jalajanakavemba hesaru rUDhiyalli yAva anilavannu
gurutisuttadeyO A anilada bEre bEre guNadharmagaLa AdhArada
mEle mAtravE A padada arthavannu sariyAgi mattu spaSTavAgi vivarisi
hELalu sAdhya.

pratyayaviruva padagaLu hesarisuva vidhAnadalli baLakeyAguttive
yAdare, avakke artha hELabEkiddarU nAvu idE samasyeyannu
edurisabEkAguttade. udAharaNegAgi, anjike, nambike, hodike,
hELike, moLake, hiDike modalAda nAmapadagaLu ike emba pratyaya
vannu anju, nambu, hode, hELu, moLe, hiDi modalAda bEre
bEre kriyApadagaLige sErisuvudara mUlaka siddhavAgive. I ellA
padagaLadU oLaracane ondE rItiyadAgideyAdarU ivugaLigiruva
artha ondE rItiyadAgilla.

I padagaLalli kelavakke avugaLa angavAgi baruva kriyApadakke
sambandhisidantaha bhAvArthavide (udA: nambike); Adare, innu kelavakke
antaha kriyeyalli baLasuva (udA: hodike, hiDike) illavE antaha
kriyeyinda dorakuva (udA: moLake) viSiSTavAda vastugaLannu
gurutisuva arthavide (4.3.(1) nODi). hAgAgi, jODupadagaLa
hAge hesarisuva vidhAnavannu baLasuvantaha pratyayaviruva padagaLigU


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


artha hELabEkiddalli, bhASeyalli avugaLa baLakeyantahadu embudannu
tiLiyuvudu atyavaSya.

I kAraNakkAgi, hesarisuva padagaLa sariyAda arthavannu bhASA
SAstrajYaru mAtravE nirdharisi hELaballaru. bhASeyannu baLasuva itara
janarige A artha tiLidideyAdarU avara tiLuvaLike miduLinalli arivige
bAradantaha (AdarU padagaLa prayOgavannu sariyAgi mADalu
sahAyakavAguvantaha) sthitiyalliruttade.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa artha Urininda Urige mattu jAti
yinda jAtige bEre bErAgiralu sAdhyavide. kAladinda kAlakkU idu
vyatyAsagoLLuttA hOguttade. Adare varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLa
artha I rIti UrindUrige vyatyAsagoLLuvudilla. udAharaNegAgi,
biLisIre emba padagucchakke ellA UrugaLallU 'beLLagina baNNaviruva
sIre' emba ondE arthavide. varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLa arthadalli
prAdESika illavE sAmAjika vyatyAsagaLu kANisikoLLabEkiddalli
sAmAnyavAgi avugaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa
arthadalli antaha prAdESika illavE sAmAjika vyatyAsagaLira
bEkAguttade.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLalli rUDhanAma mattu ankitanAmagaLendu
eraDu vidhaviddu, ivugaLa naDuve arthadalli kelavu vyatyAsagaLive
yembudannu munde (3.5)ralli nODaliruvevu. Adare I eraDu
rItiya nAmapadagaLigU artha hELalu avu entaha vyakti, vastu,
modalAduvannu gurutisuttave embudannu tiLidukoLLuvudu avaSya.

## 3.3.4 parimitiyalli vyatyAsa
hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU mattu varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLigU
naDuviruva innondu mukhya vyatyAsavEnendare, bhASeyondaralli baLake
yalliruva hesarisuva nAmapadagaLige avugaLa sankhyeya maTTige ondu
parimitiyide, Adare varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLige intaha parimiti
yilla. hosa hosa sandarbhagaLalli hosa hosa varNanegaLannu
mAtanADuvavanE racisikoLLabEkAguvudAda kAraNa ondu bhASeyalli
varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLu iSTE iveyembudAgi avugaLa sankhyeya
mEle ondu parimitiyannirisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.

idallade mAtanADuvavana kalpanASaktiyannanusarisi, hosa hosa
rItiya varNanegaLannu tayArisi hELalu ellA bhASegaLallU


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


AspadaviddE iruttade. I kAraNakkAgiyU varNisuva nAmapadagaLa
sankhye aparimitavAdudendu hELuva avaSyakateyide.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannU hosadAgi racisikoLLalu sAdhyavide
yEnO nija. Adare, I rIti avannu racisikoLLuvudu ondu
bhASeyallAguva badalAvaNeyannu sUcisuttadallade adara dinanityada
baLakeyannalla. bhASeyondannu baLasuttiruva samayadalli, adaralli
AgalE racitavAgi rUDhige bandiruva nAmapadagaLannu mAtravE A
bhASeya 'hesarisuva nAmapada'gaLendu parigaNisalu sAdhya. intaha
nAmapadagaLa sankhyege ondu parimitiyide. bASeyannu baLasuvavara
nenapinalli uLiyaballaSTu nAmapadagaLu mAtra I vidhAnada mUlaka
prayuktavAgaballuvAdudarinda bhASeyannu baLasuvavara nenapina
SaktiyE I sankhyege parimitiyannu tandoDDuttade.

Adare idu iDI samAjada nenapina Saktiyannavalambisiruttadallade
obba vyaktiya nenapina Saktiyannalla. yAkendare I nenapina Sakti ondu
bhASeyannu baLasuva ellA janarallU ondE rItiyadAgiruvudilla.
kelavarige heccu nenapina Saktiyiruttade mattu kelavarige kaDimeyiruttade.
hAgAgi, kelavarige jAsti hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa jYAnaviruttade, mattu
kelavarige kaDime padagaLa jYAnaviruttade. nenapina Sakti kaDime iruvavaru
tamage tiLiyadiruva mattu bhASeyalli baLakeyalliruva nAmapadagaLannu
bErArAdarU baLasidAga avugaLa arthavEnembudannu bEreyavarinda
kELi tiLidukoLLabEkAguttade, illavE A bhASege arthakOSa, vastu
kOSa modalAdavugaLiddalli avugaLalli nODi
tiLidukoLLabEkAguttade.

idallade, bEre bEre vyavahAragaLalliruva janaralli bEre bEre
rItiya hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu baLakeyalliddu, I viSayadallU
ondE bhASeyannADuva janaroLage vyatyAsa tOribaruttade. udA
haraNegAgi, samudrada badiyalli vAsisuva mInugArara mAtinalli
mInige mattu samudrakke sambandhisida hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu jAsti
iruttave, mattu kADinalli bETeyADi badukuva bETegArara mAtinalli
kADige mattu bETege sambandhisida hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu jAsti
iruttave. intaha vyatyAsagaLAvuvU varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLalli
kANisuvudilla.

bEre bEre SAstragaLige sambandhisidantaha hesarisuva nAmapadagaLU
bEre bErAgiddu, ivannu AyA SAstragaLannu kaliyuvavaru nenapinalli


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


irisikoLLabEkAguttade. intaha hesarisuva nAmapadagaLige 'pAribhASika
pada'gaLemba hesaride. I padagaLannu avu hesarisuva vastugaLannu kanDu
hiDidAga illavE tayArisidAga utpAdisi baLakege taralAgittu. intaha
padagaLannella sangrahisi, bEre bEre SAstragaLige bEre bEre pAribhASika
padagaLa 'kOSa'gaLannu racisalu sAdhyavideyembudarinda, antaha
hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU ondu parimitiyideyemba viSaya spaSTa
vAguttade. Adare, I SAstragaLalli baLakeyAguva varNisuva nAmapada
gucchagaLige intaha parimitiyilla, mattu avannu arthakOSagaLalli
sangrahisuva avaSyakateyU illa sAdhyateyU illa.

## 3.3.5 badalAvaNeyalli vyatyAsa
bhASeyalli kAladinda kAlakke naDeyuva badalAvaNegaLu adaralli baLake
yAguva nAmapadagaLannU bAdhisuttave. Adare I badalAvaNegaLu
entahavu emba viSayadalli hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU mattu varNi
suva nAmapadagucchagaLigU naDuve halavAru vyatyAsagaLive. I vyatyAsa
gaLigU avugaLa tayArike mattu baLakegaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLE
kAraNa embudannu gamanisabahudu.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLige artha hELalu avugaLa oLaracane
mukhyavalla. avu rUDhiyalli entaha vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLige
anvayisuttave embudu mukhya embudannu nAvu mEleyE
nODiruvevu. I kAraNakkAgi, avugaLa oLaracaneyannu badalAgadante
uLisikoLLuva avaSyakateyilla. idallade, hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannu
nenapinalliTTukonDu baLasabEkAgideyAda kAraNa, avu sankSiptavAgi
iddaSTU baLakege anukUla.

hAgAgi, antaha nAmapadagaLu samaya kaLedantella badalAvaNegaLa
mUlaka sankSiptagoLLuttA hOguvudannu nAvu kANabahudu. pratyaya
viruva padagaLalliruva pratyaya mattu padagaLu oTTusEri, pratyayada
gurutilladantAguttade, mattu jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva
padagaLu ondAgi, avu bEre bEre padagaLAgidduvemba viSayavE
gOcarakke baradantAguttade. intaha padagaLa angagaLalli yAvudAdarU
ondu sankSiptagonDu pratyayada hAge kANisatoDaguvudU intaha
badalAvaNegaLallondu.

udAharaNegAgi, heggaDe, hejjenu, heddAri, hebbAvu
modalAda padagaLalli hiri emba pada (per embudu idara haLeya


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


rUpa) modalaneya angavAgi bandideyemba viSaya I padagaLa
cAritrika adhyayanadinda spaSTavAguttade. Adare, I padagaLa
arthavEnembudannu tiLiyalu ivugaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu
illavE A racane yalli hiri emba pada bandideyembudannu tiLiyuva
avaSyakateyilla. hAgAgi, avu mEle sUcisidantaha badalAvaNegaLige
oLagAgalu sAdhyavAgide. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, doDDa mane, doDDa
mara, doDDa hAvu modalAda varNisuva padagucchagaLalli angavAgi
baruva doDDa emba pada I rIti sankSiptagoLLade pratyEkavAgiyE
uLiyabEkAgu ttade.

varNisuva padagucchagaLa arthavEnembudannu avugaLa oLaracane
yinda mAtravE tiLidukoLLalu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, avugaLa oLa
racane yAvAgalU spaSTavAgi tiLiyuvantirabEkAguttade. I kAraNa
kkAgi, avu yAvAgalU nAmapadagucchagaLAgiyE uLiyuttavallade
padagaLAgi sankSiptagoLLuvudilla. avannu bAdhisuva badalAvaNegaLendare,
avugaLa oLaracaneyalli kANisuva bEre bEre rItiya padagaLannu mattu
pratyayagaLannu vayyaktikavAgi bAdhisuva badalAvaNegaLu mattu avugaLa
racaneyalli baruva niyamagaLannu bAdhisuva badalAvaNegaLu mAtra.

## 3.3.6 oLaracaneya niyamagaLalli vyatyAsa
hesarisuva nAmapadagaLigU mattu varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLigU
naDuve avugaLa oLaracaneyalli baruva niyamagaLa maTTigU halavAru
vyatyAsagaLu kANisuttave. varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLa racaneyalli
baruva niyamagaLu vyavasthitavAgiddu, kelavE kelavu sArvatrika niyama
gaLa mUlaka I padagucchagaLa racaneyannu vivarisi hELalu sAdhyavide.

Adare hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa racaneyalli halavAru niyamagaLu
baLakeyalliddu, avugaLalli heccinavU bahaLa avyavasthitavAgiruttave
mattu toDaku toDakAgiruttave. halavAru nAmapadagaLige avugaLavE
Ada viSiSTa niyamagaLa avaSyakateyiddu, avugaLa racane
aniyamitavendE hELalU baruttade.

mEleyE tiLisiruvante, hesarisuva nAmapadagaLa oLaracane avugaLa
arthavannu tiLidukoLLuvalli avaSyavAdudalla mattu avannu hAgeyE
nenapinalli irisikonDu baLasabEkAguttade emba I eraDu viSayagaLu
avugaLa oLaracane mEle sUcisida hAge bhASeyallAguva bEre bEre
badalAvaNegaLa mUlaka kliSTavAguttA hOgalu sAdhyavAguvante


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


mADuttave. varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLannu pratiyondu bAri baLasu
vAgalU hosadAgi tayArisikoLLabEkAgideyAda kAraNa, mattu
avugaLa arthavannu nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneyindalE sAdhisikoLLa
bEkAguvudAda kAraNa, avu intaha badalAvaNegaLige oLagAgadiruttave.

udAharaNegAgi pUrvada haLegannaDadalli hosagannaDada hiriya
emba pada piriya endittu. eraDaneya akSaradalli (ri embudaralli)
ikAra bandudarindAgi A padada modalaneya akSarada ekAra ikAra
vAyitu mattu hAgAgi adu haLegannaDadalli piriya endAyitu.
anantara adara modalaneya akSaradalliruva pakAra hakAravAduda
rindAgi adu anantara hosagannaDadalli hiriya endAyitu.

hosagannaDada nAmapadagucchagaLallella idu I hiriya emba hosa
rUpadallE baruttade (udA: hiriya maga, hiriya vidvAmsaru,
ityAdi). Adare kelavu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLalli idu ivattigU
adara haLeya rUpavannu svalpamaTTige uLisikonDide. udAharaNegAgi,
hebbAvu emba padada eraDanE akSaradalli ikAravillada kAraNa,
modalaneya akSarada ekAra badalAgade hAgeyE uLidide. idallade
eraDanE akSaradallidda rakAravu mUranE akSarada vyanjanadoDane sEri
samAnateyannu paDedide. hebbAvu emba I padadoDane heddAri,
hejjenu, heggaDe modalAda padagaLannu hOlisi nODidAga I
eraDaneya viSaya spaSTavAguttade.

idE rItiyalli haLegannaDada pakAra hakAravAgade uLidiruvantaha
bEre kelavu baLakegaLu aniyamitavAgi hesarisuva nAmapadagaLalli
kANisikoLLuttave. kaypiDi emba padadalli hiDi emba padavu piDi emba
adara haLeya rUpadallE uLidide. kambani embudarallU hani emba
pada adare haLeya pakAravannu hakAravAgi mADikoLLade bakAravAgi
mADi uLisikonDide. hombaNNa, bengAvalu modalAda padagaLa
angagaLAgi bandiruva honnu, bennu modalAda padagaLu avugaLa
haLeya EkAkSara rUpadallE uLidive. hosagannaDadalli ivu ukArada
sErikeyindAgi eraDakSaradavugaLAgive mattu honnina baNNa, bennina
kAvalu modalAda varNisuva nAmapadagucchagaLalli I hosa
eraDakSarada rUpagaLE kANisikoLLuttave.

## 3.3.7 nAmapadagaLu mattu nAmapadagucchagaLu

© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisu
vudakkAgi nAvu nAmapadagucchagaLannu baLasuttEvallade bariya nAmapada
gaLannu baLasuvudilla embudannu mEleyE nODiruvevu. bariya
nAmapadagaLannu varNisuva kAryadalli baLasaballevAdarU, vyakti, vastu
modalAduvannu 'gurutisa'bEkAdAgalella avannu hesarisuva vidhAna
dalli mAtravE baLasuvudu rUDhi. I kAraNakkAgi, mEle nAmapada
mattu nAmapadagucchagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsavemmtahadu embudannu
tiLiyuvudara mUlaka, hesarisuva vidhAnakkU mattu varNisuva
vidhAnakkU naDuvina vyatyAsagaLentahavu embudannu tiLiyalu sAdhya
vAgittu.

Adare hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu
gurutisalu kannaDadalli bariya nAmapadagaLannu mAtravallade nAmapada
gucchagaLannU baLasalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, hUvina giDa emba
nAmapadagucchada baLakeyannu pariSIlisabahudu. I padagucchada mUlaka
nAvu ondu viSiSTavAda jAtige sErida giDavannu (endare adara
hUvina andakkAgi sAkuva giDavannu) gurutisuttEve. hUvina giDadalli
ellA samayagaLallU hUvirabEkendEnilla. A jAtige sErida giDa
vondaralli hUvE AgadiralU sAdhyavide.

I kAraNagaLindAgi, I nAmapadagucchavannu, mattu intahavE
bEre halavAru nAmapadagucchagaLannu hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka
vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvavugaLendu hELabEkallade
varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka gurutisuvavugaLendu hELalu sAdhya
vAgadu. hUvillada illavE hUvE Agada giDavannu hUvina giDavendu
'varNisalu' sAdhyavillavAda kAraNa hUvina giDa embudu ondu giDada
varNaneyAgalAradu.

I rIti, hesarisuva vidhAna mattu varNisuva vidhAnagaLemba I
eraDu vidhAnagaLallU nAmapadagucchagaLannu baLasalu sAdhyavide. Adare,
I eraDu vidhAnagaLalli baLakeyAguva nAmapadagucchagaLa naDuve oLa
racaneyalli kelavu vyatyAsagaLive. udAharaNegAgi, eraDu nAmapada
gaLannu a emba pratyayada mUlaka sambandhisi padagucchagaLannu
tayArisalu sAdhyavideyaSTe. intaha nAmapadagucchagaLannu hesarisuva
vidhAnadallU baLasabahudu mattu varNisuva vidhAnadallU baLasa
bahudu. Adare I eraDu rItiya baLakegaLa naDuve avu yAva
arthadalli sambandhitavAguttave embudaralli vyatyAsavide. keLage


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


koTTiruva nAmapadagucchagaLannu hOlisi nODidAga I viSaya spaSTa
vAguttade.

1. SaSThi sambandhada artha hesarisuva vidhAna varNisuva vidhAna
2. (ka) Akara hAlina koDa koDada hAlu
3. pustakada kapATu kapATina pustaka
4. (kha) anga hUvina giDa giDada hUvu
5. bAlada huLa huLada bAla
6. (ga) oDetana haNada muduka mudukana haNa
7. Toppiya huDuga huDugana Toppi
8. (gha) guNadharma baNNada ciTTe ciTTeya baNNa
9. dhayryada huDuga huDugana dhayrya
10. (i) bhAvane hedarikeya huDuga huDugana hedarike
11. prItiya henDati henDatiya prIti

mEle eraDanE kAlannalli koTTiruva nAmapadagucchagaLannu
hesarisuva vidhAnadallU mattu mUranE kAlannalli koTTiruva nAma
padagucchagaLannu varNisuva vidhAnadallU vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu
gurutisalu baLasuvudu rUDhi. udAharaNegAgi, I hUvina giDadalli
hUvE illa ennabahudu Adare nEravAgi I giDada hU giDaddalla
ennalu sAdhyavAgadu ('kAgadada hUvondannu I giDakke sikkisiddAre'
embantaha viSiSTavAda arthadalli mAtra antaha prayOga sAdhya).
giDada hU emba padagucchavannu sAmAnyavAgi varNisuva vidhAnadalli
baLasuvudE jAsti embudE idakke kAraNa.

I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagucchagaLa naDuve bandiruva a emba
pratyaya entaha sambandhavannu sUcisuttade emba viSayadalli vyatyAsa
videyembudannu gamanisabahudu. udAharaNegAgi (ka)dalli bandiruva
modalaneya kAlanna hAlina koDa mattu pustakada kapATu
emberaDu nAmapadagucchagaLu vastugaLa mUlaka avannirisuva
AkaragaLannu gurutisuvuvAdare, adE sAlina mUraneya kAlannalli


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


bandiruva koDada hAlu mattu kapATina pustaka emberaDu nAma
padagucchagaLu AkaragaLa mUlaka avugaLallirisuva vastugaLannu gurutisu
ttave. I eraDu rItiya Akara sambandhagaLalli modalaneyadannu
sAmAnyavAgi hesarisuvudakkU mattu eraDaneyadannu varNisuvudakkU
baLasuva rUDhi kannaDadallide.

mEle koTTiruva itara nAmapadagucchagaLalliyU idE rItiya
viruddha prayOgagaLiruvudannu kANabahudu. (kha)dalli bandiruva
hUvina giDa mattu bAlada huLa emberaDu padagucchagaLu angagaLa
mUlaka A angagaLannu hondiruva sasya mattu prANigaLannu gurutisu
vuvAdare, avugaLa eduru koTTiruva giDada hU mattu huLada bAla
emberaDu padagucchagaLu angagaLannu hondiruva sasya mattu prANigaLa
mUlaka avugaLa angagaLannu gurutisuttave. ivugaLalli modalaneya
vannu hesarisuvudakkAgiyU mattu eraDaneyadannu varNisuvu
dakkAgiyU baLasuvudu kannaDadalli rUDhiyAgide.

idE rItiyalli vastuvina oDeyanannu vastuvininda gurutisuva
padagucchavannu (udA: haNada muduka mattu Toppiya huDuga)
hesarisuvudakkAgiyU mattu oDeyaninda vastuvannu gurutisuva pada
gucchavannu (udA: mudukana haNa mattu huDugana Toppi)
varNisuvudakkAgiyU baLasuvudannu oDetanavemba sambandhavannu
tOrisuva (ga)da sAlugaLalli kANabahudu, guNadharmadinda guNa
dharmavuLLudannu gurutisuva padagucchavannu (udA: baNNada ciTTe
mattu dhayryada huDuga) hesarisuvudakkAgiyU mattu guNadharma
vuLLudarinda guNadharmavannu gurutisuva padagucchavannu (udA:
ciTTeya baNNa mattu huDugana dhayrya) varNisuvudakkAgiyU
baLasu vudannu guNadharmavemba sambandhavannu tOrisuva (gha)da
sAlugaLalli kANabahudu mattu bhAvaneyinda bhAvisuvavanannu
gurutisuva pada gucchavannu (udA: hedarikeya huDuga mattu
prItiya henDati) hesarisuvudakkAgiyU mattu bhAvisuvavaninda
bhAvaneyannu gurutisuva padagucchavannu (udA: huDugana hedarike
mattu henDatiya prIti) varNisuvudakkAgi baLasuvudannu
bhAvaneyemba sambandhavannu tOrisuva (i)da sAlugaLalli
kANabahudu.

Adare I eraDu rItiya viruddha sambandhagaLalli baruva padaguccha
gaLa baLake aSTondu kaTTuniTTinadEnalla. eraDanE kAlannalli baruva


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


padagucchagaLannu hesarisuva vidhAnadalli mAtravallade varNisuva vidhAna
dallU baLasalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi dhayryada huDuga emba
padaguccha dhayryada huDugana dhayryavella ingihOgide emba
vAkyadalli obba huDuganannu varNisuva badalu hesarisuttiruva hAge
kANisuttade. idE rItiyalli mUranE kAlannalli baruva padaguccha
gaLalli kelavannu hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka baLasalU sAdhyavide. Adare
antaha prayOgagaLu bahaLa kaDime.

## 3.4 vibhajaneya kelavu samasyegaLu
kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu nirdharisalu
horaDuva modalu nAmapadagaLannu itara vAkyAmSagaLinda (adarallU
nAmapadagucchagaLinda) pratyEkisuvudu avaSya embudannu mEle
nODiddevu. hIge pratyEkisuvalli kelavu samasyegaLive. sAmAnyavAgi
nAmapadagaLu hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlakavU mattu nAmapada
gucchagaLu varNisuva vidhAnada mUlakavU vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu
gurutisuttave. hAgAgi I vyatyAsada AdhArada mEle averaDannu heccina
sandarbhagaLallU pratyEkisi hELalu sAdhyavide.

Adare mEle sUcisidante, kelavondu sandarbhagaLalli nAmapada
gucchagaLannU hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka gurutisuva kAryadalli
baLasalu sAdhyavide. intaha sandarbhagaLalli I eraDu rItiya
vAkyAmSagaLannu vAkyadalli avu naDesuva kelasavEnu embudara
sahAyadinda bErpaDisalu sAdhyavAgadu.

nAmapada mattu nAmapadagucchagaLa naDuve avugaLa heccina
baLakegaLallU kANisuva innondu vyatyAsavEnendare, nAmapadagucchagaLa
angagaLAgi baruva padagaLu bEre bErAgiruttave mattu avugaLalli
ondaroDane innondannu sambandhisalu padarUpa pratyayagaLu (udA:
a emba pratyaya) baLakeyAgiruttave. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, nAmapadagaLa
angagaLAgi baruva padagaLu oTTu sEri ondE padavAgiruttave, mattu
avugaLa naDuve pratyayagaLAvuvU baruvudilla. hAgEnAdarU pratyaya
gaLu baruvudiddarU avu padapratyayagaLAgiruttavallade padarUpa
pratyayagaLAgiruvudilla.

Adare nAmapadagaLannu nAmapadagucchagaLinda pratyEkisalu I rIti
oLaracaneyannu ellA sandarbhagaLallU baLasalu sAdhyavAgadu. udA
haraNegAgi, kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLondige guNapadagaLannu baLasuvAga


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


avakke padarUpa pratyayagaLannu sErisuva avaSyakateyilla. guNapadagaLu
nEravAgi nAmapadagaLa munde bandu nilluttave. kempu gODe, kappu
baNNa, doDDa mane modalAda nAmapadagucchagaLalli I rIti padaga
LeraDu padarUpa pratyayagaLa sahAyavillade nEravAgi sambandhita
vAgiruvudannu kANabahudu. intaha vAkyAmSagaLu nAmapadagucchagaLE
athavA bariya nAmapadagaLE (endare jODupadagaLE) emba viSaya
dalli sandigdhateyunTAgalu sAdhyavide.

udAharaNegAgi, bisinIru emba vAkyAmSadalli bisi emba guNa
padavannu nIru emba nAmapadadondige baLasalAgide. ivugaLa naDuve
padarUpa pratyayavAvudU illa. hAgAgi illi angagaLAgi bandiruva
padagaLu bEre bErAgiveyE (endare idu ondu nAmapadagucchavE)
athavA oTTu sEri ondE padavAgi bandiveyE (endare idu
jODupadavE) embudannu I padada oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle
mAtravE nirdharisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. I vAkyAmSavannu yAva
rItiyalli baLasalAgide mattu baLasuvavana ASayavEnu embudannu
tiLiyuva mUlaka mAtravE intaha sandarbhagaLalli ondu nirdhArakke
baralu sAdhya.

bisinIru emba vAkyAmSakke kannaDadalli nAmapadagucchavAgiyU
baLakeyide mattu bariya nAmapada (jODupada)vAgiyU baLakeyide.
adakke 'beccagiruva nIru' emba arthavideyAdare adannu ondu nAma
padagucchavendU mattu 'omme bisimADida (endare kudisi Arisida)
nIru' emba arthavideyAdare jODupadavendU hELabahudu.
modalaneyadu ondu vastuvannu varNisuttade mattu eraDaneyadu
hesarisuttade. intaha arthasandigdhategaLiruvalli sAmAnyavAgi baLakeya
sandarbhagaLE sariyAda arthavannu odagisikoDuttave. udAharaNegAgi,
snAna mADalu horaTavanu bisinIru bEkendu hELidalli beccagina
nIru bEkemba ASaya ADuganadAgirabEkAda kAraNa, illi bisinIru
embudannu ondu varNaneyendu hELabEkAguttade. Adare, UTakke
kuLitavanu bisinIru bEkendu hELidalli sAmAnyavAgi kuDiyalu
bisimADi taNisiruva (endare byAkTIriyAgaLannu nASapaDisiruva) nIru
bEkembudAgi ADugana ASayavirabEkAda kAraNa, bisinIru embudu
illi ondu hesarisuva nAmapadavAgi (jODupadavAgi) bandideyendu
hELabEkAguttade.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


## 3.5 hesarisuva nAmapadagaLalli vayvidhya
hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannu bEre bEre rItiyalli bEre bEre tatvagaLa
AdhArada mEle vibhajisalu sAdhyavide. ivugaLalli rUDhanAma mattu
ankitanAmagaLemba vibhajane atyanta prAmukhyavAdudu. idu nAma
padagaLu avu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLondige yAva
rItiyalli sambandhitavAgive, endare avakke A hesarugaLu hEge bandive
embudara mEle avalambiside. ankitanAmagaLu avu hesarisuva vyakti,
vastu modalAdavugaLalli pratiyondakkU bEre bErAgi sambandhita
vAgiruvuvAdare, rUDhanAmagaLu antahavugaLigella ondE bArige
sambandhitavAgiruttave (vivaragaLige 3.5.1 nODi).

sAmAnyavAgi ankitanAmagaLannu mAtravE 'hesaru' emba padada
mUlaka gurutisuvudu rUDhi. Adare I pustakadalli hesarisu emba
padavannu varNisu emba padakke edurAgi nillisiruva kAraNa, hesaru
emba padakke I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLannU gurutisuvantaha
artha bandide. idannu hesarisu mattu hesaru emba padagaLa pAri
bhASika prayOgavendu parigaNisabahudu.

hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannu avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mElU
vibhajisalu sAdhyavide. Adare I vibhajane mEle koTTiruva
rUDhanAma-ankitanAma emba vibhajaneyannu aDDakke kattarisuttade. I
vibhajaneyalli yAva oLaracaneyannU tOrisadiruva nIru, giDa, mara,
sIte modalAdavugaLadu ondu vibhAgavAdare, yAvudAdarU ondu
pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka siddhavAda 'pratyayaviruva' nAma
padagaLadu (udA: anjike, kuNita, aLivu, taTTe ityAdi) innondu
vibhAga, mattu eraDu (athavA jAsti) padagaLa sErikeyinda (endare
samAsadinda) siddhavAda 'jODupada'gaLadu (udA: kasabarike,
kaNNIru, doDDamma, kaygamba ityAdi) mattondu vibhAga.

idallade nAmapadagaLa artha, avu vAkyadalli naDesabEkAgiruva
kelasa, modalAdavugaLannAdharisiyU avannu bEre bEre pangaDagaLAgi
vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. ghaTanegaLannu hesarisuva bhAvanAmagaLu,
guNadharmagaLannu hesarisuva guNanAmagaLu, gaNya mattu agaNya
nAmapadagaLu, sajIvi mattu nirjIvi nAmapadagaLu, manuSya-
manuSyEtara nAmapadagaLu, sankhyApadagaLu, sarvanAmagaLu ityAdi
vibhajanegaLannu illi udAharisabahudu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


kriyApadagaLige kelavu pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka avu
nirdESisuva kriyeyannu hesarisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi kuNi
emba kriyApadavu nirdESisuva kriyeyannu kuNita emba nAmapada
hesarisuttade; bedaru emba kriyApadavu nirdESisuva kriyeyannu
bedarike emba nAmapadavu hesarisuttade. intaha pratyayaviruva
nAmapadagaLannu 'bhAvanAma'gaLendu kareyuva rUDhiyide.

idE rItiyalli guNapadagaLige kelavu pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara
mUlaka avu sUcisuva guNadharmagaLannu hesarisuvantaha nAmapada
gaLannu racisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi biLi emba guNapadavu
sUcisuva guNadharmavannu biLupu emba nAmapada hesarisuttade;
jANa emba guNapadavu sUcisuva guNadharmavannu jANme emba
nAmapada hesarisuttade. intaha pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLannu
'guNanAma'gaLendu kareyabahudu.

sankhyApadagaLondige baruva sAdhyateyannavalambisi nAmapadagaLannu
'gaNya' mattu 'agaNya'gaLendu eraDu vibhAgagaLAgi vingaDisalu sAdhya
vide. Adare I vibhajane rUDhanAmagaLige mAtra anvayisuttade.
ankitanAmagaLella gaNyanAmapadagaLAgi mAtravE iraballuvembudannu
munde (3.5.1)ralli nODaliruvevu.

sajIvi mattu nirjIvi embudAgi nAmapadagaLu gurutisuva vyakti,
vastu, prANi modalAduvannu eraDu mukhya vibhAgagaLalli vingaDisalu
sAdhyaviddu, avannu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannU I eraDu vibhAgagaLalli
vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. idallade, manuSya-manuSyEtara emba
innondu sajIvigaLa vibhajane mattu ganDu-heNNu emba mattondu
sajIvigaLa vibhajane - ivU kUDa kannaDada nAmapadagaLalli kANisuttave.
vAkyadalli nAmapadagaLu naDesuva kelasavannAdharisiyU avannu
bEre bEre vibhajanegaLige oLapaDisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, gaNya
vastugaLa gaNaneyalli prayuktavAguva ondu, eraDu, mUru
modalAduvannu sankhyApadagaLemba vibhAgadallU mattu mAtige
sambandhisidante bEre bEre kelasagaLannu sAdhisikoDuva vyaktigaLannu
gurutisuva nAnu, nInu, avanu, tAnu modalAduvannu
'sarvanAma'gaLemba vibhAgadallU sErisi hELalu sAdhyavide. intaha
vibhajanegaLU rUDhanAmagaLalli mAtra kANisuttave.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


nAmapadagaLa I bEre bEre rItiya vibhajanegaLalli atyanta
prAmukhyavAgiruva rUDhanAma-ankitanAma emba vibhajaneyannu I
keLage svalpa vistAravAgi pariSIlisalAgide.

## 3.6 rUDhanAmagaLu mattu ankitanAmagaLu
hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisaballa
nAmapadagaLannu rUDhanAmagaLu mattu ankitanAmagaLu emba eraDu
mukhya pangaDagaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavembudannu mEle nODiruvevu.
I eraDara naDuviruva mukhya vyatyAsavEnendare, ankitanAmagaLu avu
hesarisuva vyakti, vastu illavE sthaLagaLige pratyEka pratyEkavAgi sambandhita
vAguttave, Adare rUDhanAmagaLu antahavugaLigella ondE bArige
sambandhitavAguttave.

udAharaNegAgi basavappa emba ankitanAmavannu pariSIlisa
bahudu. ondE Urinalli I hesarinavaru halavu mandi iralu
sAdhyavide. Adare ivarellarigU ondE bArige I hesarannu koTTilla.
pratiyobbanigU bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli bEre bEre janaru I
hesaranniDalu nirdharisiruttAre. idallade, hesaru ondE AdarU I
vyaktigaLoLage bEre yAva sAmyateyU irabEkAgilla.

rUDhanAmagaLa baLake idarinda tIra bhinnavAdudu. udAharaNegAgi
baDagi emba rUDhanAmavannu pariSIlisabahudu. ondE Urinalli I
nAmapada hesarisuva vyaktigaLu halavAru mandi iralu sAdhyavide
yEnO nija. Adare, intaha vyaktigaLannella I padada mUlaka
hesarisuva nirdhAravannu kannaDa bhASeyannADuva samAjadalli
yAvAgalO omme mADirabEku. A nirdhArada phalavAgi Avattu
jIvisuttidda kelavu viSiSTa vyaktigaLannu mAtravallade munde jIvisa
liruva (mattu adakkinta hinde jIvisuttidda) antaha itara ellA
vyaktigaLannU adu hesarisuvantAyitu. I pada hesarisuva vyaktigaLoLage
ondu rItiya sAmyavU ide. avarella ondE rItiya (marada kelasa
mADuva) vxttiyalliruvavaru tAnE!.

## 3.6.1 arthadalli vyatyAsa
Adare I vyatyAsavannAdharisi rUDhanAmagaLige arthavide (A arthavu
avu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLoLage samAnavAgiruva
guNadharmavannavalambisiruttade) mattu ankitanAmagaLige (avu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa naDuve sAmyavirabEkAgilla
embudarindAgi) arthavilla endu vAdisidevAdare, adu tappAdItu.
yAkendare, eraDakkU avu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa
guNadharmagaLannAdharisi artha hELalu sAdhyavide mattu eraDakkU
nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle artha hELalu sAdhya
villa.

arthada maTTige I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa naDuviruva
vyatyAsavEnendare, ondu rUDhanAma adu hesarisuva vyakti illavE
vastugaLondige ondE bArige sambandhitavAguvudAda kAraNa,
avellavugaLigU samAnavAgiruvantaha guNadharmagaLu adara arthavAga
balluvu. Adare, ondu ankitanAma adu hesarisuva vyakti illavE
vastugaLondige bEre bErAgi sambandhitavAguvudAda kAraNa, adu
hesarisuva pratiyondu vyakti illavE vastuvigU sambandhisidante adakke
halavAru bEre bEre arthagaLiruttave. I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa
baLakegU arthada avaSyakateyideyembudannu I keLagina viSaya
spaSTapaDisuttade.

rUDhanAmada arthavannAdharisi adu hesarisuva vyakti illavE vastu
vannu gurutisalu sAdhyaviruvante, ankitanAmada arthavannAdharisi adu
hesarisuva vyakti illavE vastuvannU gurutisalu sAdhyavide. udA
haraNegAgi naLini emba ankitanAma namage paricayaviruva huDugi
yobbaLannu hesarisuvudiddalli, A huDugiya kelavu viSiSTavAda guNa
dharmagaLannu adara arthavendu parigaNisalu sAdhyavide. naLini emba
padada mUlaka nAvu A huDugiyannu bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli -
Ake langa hAkiruvAga, sIre toTTiruvAga, illavE kAyileyinda
bahaLa kxSavAgi Aspatreyalli malagiruvAga gurutisabEkiddalli I viSiSTa
guNadharmagaLu, endare naLini emba padakke nAvu koDabahudAda
artha, sahAyakavAguttade.

huDugi emba rUDhanAmakkU adu hesarisuva vyaktigaLalli
kANisuva kelavu viSiSTavAda guNadharmagaLa AdhArada mEle artha
hELabEkAguttade, mattu I vyaktigaLannu bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli
huDugi emba hesarina mUlaka gurutisabEkAdAga I guNadharmagaLu
- endare avannAdharisi sAdhisalAgiruva huDugi emba padada artha
sahAyakke baruttade. Adare ankitanAmada hAge illi ondE vyaktiya
guNadharmada AdhArada mEle artha hELuvudilla. idakke badalu A


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


pada hesarisuva bEre bEre halavAru vyaktigaLige samAnavAgiruva
guNadharmagaLa AdhArada mEle artha hELuttEve.

Adare, ondu ankitanAma I rIti halavAru vyaktigaLannu
hesarisuttideyAdare (endare, naLini emba hesarina huDugiyaru
halavariruvarAdare) avaralli pratiyobbarigU sambandisidante A padakke
halavAru bEre bEre arthagaLannu sAdhisikoLLabEkAdItu. ankitanAma
vannu I vyaktigaLige bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli bEre bErAgi sambandhisa
lAgide mattu rUDhanAmavannu ondE sandarbhadalli ellarigU oTTAgi
sambandhisalAgide embudE I vyatyAsakke mUla kAraNa.

rUDhanAmada arthavannu nEravAgi adara oLaracaneya AdhArada
mEle sAdhisalu sAdhyavAgadembudannu mEleyE nODiruvevu.
karihalage emba rUDhanAmavu gurutisuva sAdhana kappAgiyU ira
bEkAgilla, halageyinda tayArisiddU AgabEkAgilla; UTada samaya
dalli koDuva bisinIru taNNIrigintalU taNNagAgiralu sAdhyavide;
cikkammanu prAyadalli mattu gAtradalli ammaniginta doDDavaLAgiralu
sAdhyavide; intaha halavAru udAharaNegaLannu idakke AdhAravAgi
koDabahudu.

ankitanAmada arthavannU idE rItiyalli nEravAgi avugaLa
oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle sAdhisalu sAdhyavAgadu. udAharaNegAgi,
kSIrasAgara emba hesaru (ankitanAma) iruva obba vyaktiya maneyalli
svalpavU hAlilladiralu sAdhyavide; kariyappa emba hesarina vyakti
beLLappa emba hesarina innobba vyaktiginta heccu beLLagiralu sAdhyavide;
vidyASAstri emba huDugi nAlku bAri parIkSeyalli phElAgiralu
sAdhyavide; ityAdi. I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLU hesarisuva
vidhAnada mUlaka vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvuvAda
kAraNa, avugaLa arthavannu avu gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalA
davugaLa guNadharmada AdhArada mEle mAtravE sAdhisalu sAdhya. I
viSayadalli rUDhanAma mattu ankitanAmagaLa naDuve vyatyAsavilla
embudannilli gamanisikoLLuvudu avaSya.

## 3.6.2 sambandhadalli vyatyAsa
ondu bhASeyalli baruva rUDhanAmagaLa naDuve bEre bEre rItiya
sambandhagaLannu kanDukoLLalu sAdhyavide. Adare ankitanAmagaLa naDuve
intaha sambandhagaLiruvudilla embudu I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


naDuviruva innondu mukhya vyatyAsa. idakkU kUDa rUDhanAmagaLu
tAvu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu oTTAgi hesarisuttave,
mattu ankitanAmagaLu avannu pratyEka pratyEkavAgi hesarisuttave
embudE mUla kAraNa.

obba vyakti bEre bEre vyaktigaLondige samAna guNadharmagaLannu
tOrisuttiralu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, A vyaktiyannu bEre bEre
rUDhanAmagaLa mUlaka gurutisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi obba
vyaktiyannu muduka, baDava, kuLLa, mESTru, brahmacAri, kuruDa
modalAda halavAru rUDhanAmagaLa mUlaka gurutisi hELalu sAdhya
vide. Atanige itara mudukarondige samAna guNadharmagaLiveyAdare
Atanannu muduka emba rUDhanAmadinda gurutisabahudu, mattu adE
vyaktige itara baDavarondige samAna guNadharmagaLiveyAdare Atanannu
baDava emba rUDhanAmadinda gurutisabahudu, ityAdi.

idallade, rUDhanAmagaLu gurutisuva vyaktigaLu ententaha gumpu
gaLallella sErikonDiraballaru mattu A gumpugaLa naDuve yAva yAva
rItiya sambandhagaLella ive emba viSayada AdhArada mEle avarannu
gurutisuva rUDhanAmagaLa naDuveyU bEre bEre rItiya sambandha
gaLannu kANalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, ondu rUDhanAmavu
gurutisuva vyaktigaLannella innondu rUDhanAmavU gurutisaballudAdare
(udA: navkara mattu sEvaka) antaha eraDu padagaLu
samAnArthakagaLu illavE 'paryAya' padagaLendu hELabahudu.
eraDaneya pada bEreyU kelavu vyaktigaLannu gurutisaballudAdare
(udA: ganDasu mattu manuSya) avugaLalli modalaneyadu
eraDaneyadaralli 'antargata'vAgiruva padavendu hELabahudu.

eraDu rUDhanAmagaLalli ondu gurutisuva vyaktigaLalli kelavarannu
mAtra innondu gurutisuttiddu, adu bEre kelavu vyaktigaLannU
gurutisuttideyAdare (udA: muduka mattu baDava) avugaLoLage
ondannondu 'sILuva' sambandhavideyendu hELabahudu. mattu eraDu
rUDhanAmagaLu gurutisuva vyaktigaLu bhinna bhinnarAgiruvarAdare (udA:
ganDasu mattu hengasu) avugaLa naDuve 'asangata' sambandhavide
yendu hELabahudu.

Adare, ankitanAmagaLa naDuve I rIti bEre bEre rItiya
sambandhagaLannu kANalu sAdhyavAgadu. heccina ankitanAmagaLigU avu
gurutisuva vyaktigaLu (illavE vastugaLu) halaviruvudu nijavAdarU


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


intaha vyakti illavE vastugaLoLage sAmyavEnU irabEkAgilla. I
niyamakke kelavu apavAdagaLiveyEnO nija. udAharaNegAgi,
ganDasarannu mattu hengasarannu gurutisuva ankitanAmagaLu sAmAnya
vAgi bEre bErAgiruttave. jAnaki emba hesarannu ganDasarigAgalI
illavE rAju emba hesarannu hengasarigAgalI koTTiruvudannu nAvu
kANuvudilla. hAgAgi, I eraDu rItiya padagaLa naDuve 'asangata'
emba sambandhavideyendu vAdisalu sAdhyavide.

Adare I niyamakke apavAdagaLiralU sAdhyavide. illi gamanisa
bEkAgiruva mukhyavAda amSavEnendare, ankitanAmagaLa baLakege avu
gurutisuva bEre bEre vyaktigaLa illavE vastugaLa naDuve sAmyaviruva
avaSyakateyilla, mattu hAge iddarU adu avugaLa tayArike mattu
baLakeya hindiruva mUla tatvagaLinda sAdhitavAdudalla.

## 3.6.3 gaNya mattu aganya
rUDhanAmagaLannu gaNya mattu agaNyavendu eraDu vidhavAgi vingaDisalu
sAdhyavide. gaNyanAmagaLu gurutisuva vastugaLannu ondu, eraDu,
mUru, nAlku embudAgi lekka hAki hELalu sAdhyavide (udA:
bAlehaNNu) mattu agaNyanAmagaLu gurutisuva vastugaLannu I rIti
lekka hAki hELalu sAdhyavilla (udA: nIru) embudE I eraDu
rItiya rUDhanAmagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa. gaNyanAmagaLu gurutisuva
vastugaLu namma kaNNige kANisuvante pratyEka pratyEkavAda astitvaviruva
halavu vastugaLa samudAyavAgiruvudE idakke kAraNa.

Adare, ankitanAmagaLannu I rIti gaNya mattu agaNya embudAgi
vingaDisalu sAdhyavAgadu. avugaLa mUlaka sAmAnyavAgi gaNyavastu
gaLannu mAtravE gurutisalAguttade embudE idakke kAraNa. idu I
eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa naDuviruva innondu mukhyavAda
vyatyAsavendu hELabahudu. nIrinantaha agaNyavastugaLu avugaLa
pAtregaLa AdhArada mEle pratyEkateyannu paDedu gaNyavastugaLAdAga
mAtra avannu ankitanAmagaLa mUlaka gurutisalu sAdhyavAdItu.
udAharaNegAgi ondu nadiyAgi hariyuva nIrannu kAvEri emba
ankitanAmada mUlaka gurutisaballevu mattu ondu dESavAgi nilluva
maNNannu bhArata emba ankitanAmada mUlaka gurutisaballevu, ityAdi.

ankitanAmagaLannu avu gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLige
pratyEka pratyEkavAgi anvayisabEkAgideyAda kAraNa mattu agaNya vastu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


gaLu I rIti pratyEka pratyEkavAgi oDedukonDillavAda kAraNa,
ankitanAmagaLu agaNyavastugaLige hesarugaLAgi baruvudillavendu hELa
bahudu. hIge I mUraneya mukhya vyatyAsavU I eraDu rItiya
nAmapadagaLu yAva rItiyalli avu gurutisuva vastugaLondige
sambandhisuttave embudara mEle avalambitavAgide.

## 3.7 sArAmSa
nAmapada illavE nAmapadagucchagaLannu prAmukhyavAgi vyakti, vastu,
viSaya modalAdavugaLannu gurutisuvudakkAgi vAkyagaLalli baLasuttEve.
I gurutisuva kelasavannu hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu emba
eraDu bEre bEre vidhAnagaLa mUlaka naDesalu sAdhyavide. sAmAnya
vAgi, nAmapadagaLu hesarisuva vidhAnadallU mattu nAmapadagucchagaLu
varNisuva vidhAnadallU baLakeyAguttave. Adare kelavu viSiSTavAda
nAmapadagucchagaLu hesarisuva vidhAnadallU baLakeyAgaballuvu. ida
llade, varNisuva vidhAnadalli kriyApadagaLa mattu guNapadagaLa kelavu
rUpagaLU baraballuvu.

kelavu sandarbhagaLalli nAmapadagaLannu nAmapadagucchagaLinda pratyE
kisuvudu svalpa kaSTavendu tOrabahudu. Adare hesarisuva vidhAnadalli
baLakeyAguva padakkU mattu varNisuva vidhAnadalli baLakeyAguva
padaguccha illavE padarUpakkU naDuve halavu vyatyAsagaLiddu, I
ellA vyatyAsagaLannU AdhAravAgirisikonDu avannu bErpaDisalu
sAdhya. padagaLa oLaracaneyannu varNisuva I pustakadalli hesarisuva
vidhAna dalli baLakeyAguva padagaLannu mAtra pariSIlisuva
avaSyakateyide. varNisuva vidhAnadalli baruva padagucchagaLu mattu
padarUpagaLu vAkyaracaneya niyamakke anusAravAgi tayArAguva
kAraNa, avannu vAkyagaLa oLaracaneyemba bErondu pustakadalli
pariSIlisabahudu.

hesarisuva vidhAnadalli baruva padagaLannu bEre bEre rItiyalli
vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. ivugaLalli rUDhanAma mattu ankitanAma emba
vingaDane bahaLa prAmukhyavAdudu. ankitanAmagaLalli pratiyondannU
avu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu, sthAna modalAdavugaLige pratyEka
pratyEkavAgi anvayisalAgide, mattu rUDhanAmagaLalli pratiyondannU
avu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLige ondE bArige anvayisa


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


lAgide embudE I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa naDuviruva mukhya
vyatyAsa.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-4) | [English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-4--nouns-with-suffixes)

## adhyAya nAlkupratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLu

## 4.1 pIThike
kannaDadalli mukhyavAgi mUru rItiya pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLu
baLakeyallive. ivu anukramavAgi nAmapada, kriyApada mattu
guNapadagaLige ondu athavA jAsti pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara
mUlaka tayArAgiruttave. udAharaNegAgi gANiga emba
pratyayaviruva nAma padavu gANa emba nAmapadakke iga emba
pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAgide; agalike emba
nAmapadavu agalu emba kriyA padakke ike emba pratyayavannu
sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAgide; mattu baDava emba nAmapadavu
baDa emba guNapadakke va emba pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka
tayArAgide.

I mUru rItiya pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLalli kriyApadagaLige
pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArAgiruva eraDaneya rItiya nAmapadagaLE
kannaDadalli jAsti. Adare kelavu sandarbhagaLalli intaha nAmapadagaLannu
kriyApadagaLige pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyE athavA adE
rUpada nAmapadagaLige pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyE
endu spaSTavAgi hELalu sAdhyavAgadiruvudU ide. udAharaNegAgi
hiDike emba nAmapadavannu hiDi (udA: kattiyannu hiDi) emba
kriyApadadindalAgali illavE adE rUpada hiDi (udA: kattiya
hiDi) emba nAmapadadindalAgali tayArisiralu sAdhyavide. (hiDi emba
nAmapadadalli 'sonne' pratyayavideyendu hELuvudu (4.3.11


nODi) I samasyege vyayAkaraNigaLu kanDuhiDidiruva ondu
parihAra.)

pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLalli heccinavU ondu padakke ondu
pratyayavannu mAtra sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAdavugaLu. ondakkinta
jAsti pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisiruva nAmapadagaLa sankhye kannaDa
dalli bahaLa kaDime. tiLuvaLike embudu I rIti ondakkinta jAsti
pratyayagaLiruva nAmapada. idaralli tiLi emba kriyApadakke vaLi mattu
ike emba eraDu pratyayagaLannu sErisalAgide. intaha ondakkinta jAsti
pratyayagaLiruva nAmapadagaLalli heccinavU pratyayagaLannu ondondAgi
endare, eraDu bEre bEre staragaLalli sErisuvudara mUlaka tayA
rAgiruttave embudannu gamanisabahudu.

udAharaNegAgi mInugArike emba padadalli mInu emba nAma
padadondige gAra mattu ike emba eraDu pratyayagaLu baruvu
vAdarU adannu modalige mInu emba padakke gAra emba pratyaya
vannu sErisi mInugAra emba padavannu tayArisi, anantara A padakke
ike emba pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArisalAgideyendu
hELalu sAdhyavide. tiLuvaLike embudara hinde tiLuvaLi emba
padavilla diddarU adakke samanAgiruva hiDuvaLi, gottuvaLi
modalAdavu gaLiveyembudannu gamanisabahudu.

kannaDadalli baruva pratyayagaLellavU parapratyayagaLu, endare, nAma
pada, kriyApada illavE guNapadagaLa anantara baruvavugaLu. udA:
meccu-ge, naDa-te, aLi-vu ityAdi. pUrvapratyayagaLu endare
padagaLa modala bhAgavAgi baruva pratyayagaLu kannaDadalli bEre bhASe
gaLinda eravalAgi banda padagaLalli mAtra kANisuttave. udAharaNegAgi
samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda a-txpti, nir-bhAgya, vi-jYAna
modalAda nAmapadagaLalli a-, nir-, vi- modalAda pUrva
pratyayagaLu kANisuttave (8.3.5 nODi). idallade, hIge eravalAgi
banda padagaLalli kANisuva kelavu pUrvapratyayagaLu kannaDadavE Ada
padagaLigU anTikoLLuvudannu apa-nambike embantaha pratyayaviruva
padagaLalli aparUpavAgi kANabahudu.

ittIcege SrIdhar (1995:133,157) avaru kannaDadalli baruva
hejjenu, hingAlu, ibbadi, kemmaNNu modalAda padagaLalli
pUrvapratyayada prayOgavideyendu vAdisiddAre. sAmAnyavAgi
intaha padagaLannu jODupadagaLendU mattu avugaLa Adiyalli


baruva hej, him, in, ib, kem modalAda angagaLannu
padagaLendU parigaNisuvudu rUDhi. SrIdhar avaru idu sariyalla,
ivugaLa Adiyalli baruva angagaLu pratyayagaLallade padagaLalla endu
vAdisiddAre.

pada mattu pratyayagaLa naDuviruva vibhajane kelavondu sandarbha
gaLalli aspaSTavAgiralu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, mattu cAritrikavAgi
pratyayagaLu svatantravAgidda padagaLinda beLedu bandiralu sAdhyavide
yAda kAraNa, intaha vAdagaLige kelavomme koneyE illavendAguvu
dide. Adare I mElina vAda antahadallavendu toruttade. kannaDadalli
svatantravAgi baruva hiridu, hinde, eraDu, kempu modalAda pada
gaLigU mattu mEle koTTiruva hejjenu, hingAlu modalAda
padagaLa Adiyalli baruva angagaLigU naDuve spaSTavAda sambandhavide.
I sambandha entahadu embudannu nirdharisidAga hej, him
modalAdavugaLu pratyayagaLE athavA padagaLE emba praSnege uttara
doreyuttade.

hiridu embudaralli baruva du emba anga doDDadu, biLidu
modalAdavugaLalli kANisuva napumsaka Ekavacana pratyaya; hiri
embudu bEreDegaLalli svatantravAgi baraballa guNapada (udA: hiri
magaLu); hinde embudannu de emba pratyayada mUlaka tayArisalu
sAdhyaviddu, idaralli him emba modalaneya bhAgavE padavendu hELa
bEkAguttade; eraDu embudarallU Du embudu ondu pratyaya
mattu adara mundiruva era embudE pada; kempu embudaralli
baruva pu emba anga tampu, nuNupu, biLupu, impu modalA
davugaLalli kANisuva pratyayavAgiddu, adara mundiruva kem embudE
padavAgide.

mEle koTTiruva hejjenu, hingAlu, innUru modalAda
jODupadagaLalli I padagaLu modalaneya angavAgi bandiddu avu
hiridu, hinde, eraDu modalAdavugaLalli kANisuva pratyayagaLannu
kaLedukonDu I jODupadagaLalli bandiveyendu hELuvudE sari
yendu tOruttade. ivugaLalli hiri embudu her (hej) emba
rUpadallU mattu era embudu ir (ij, in) emba rUpadallU
baralu kannaDadalli naDeda eraDu dhvani badalAvaNegaLu kAraNa.

(1) her embudara ekAra hiri embudaralli ikAravAgide. I
padada eraDaneya akSaradalli ikAraviddudE I badalAvaNege kAraNa.


(idE badalAvaNeyannu beLLage-biLi embudarallU kANabahudu). (2)
ir embudara ikAra eraDu embudaralli ekAravAgide. I
badalAvaNege eraDu emba padada eraDaneya akSadalli akAra
bandiruvudE kAraNa (idE badalAvaNeyannu nillu-nelasu
embudarallU kANabahudu).

I sandarbhadalli ondu mukhyavAda viSayavannu gamanakke tandu
koLLuvudu avaSya. jODupadavondara oLaracaneyembudu mukhyavAgi
adara cAritrika amSagaLa mEle avalambisiruttade. adannu tayArisi
baLakege tandAga yAva guNadharmavannu ArisalAgittu mattu A
guNadharmavannu sUcisalu yAva padagaLannu baLasalAgittu embudu
adara oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu nirdharisuvalli sahAyaka
vAguttade (munde 5.5 nODi). haLegannaDadallEnE kANisuva
kemmaNNu, innUru modalAda padagaLannu cAritrikavAgi eraDu padagaLa
jODaNeyinda (samAsadinda) sulabhavAgi sAdhisalu sAdhyavideyAda
kAraNa, ivannu jODupadagaLendu parigaNisuvudaralli yAva
tondareyU illa. hAgAgi, ivugaLalli pUrvapratyayagaLiveyendu
kalpisikonDu ivannu pratyayaviruva padagaLendu hELuvudu sariyAga
lAradu.

## 4.2 pratyayagaLa svarUpa
padagaLa oLaracaneyalli baLakeyAguva padapratyayagaLalli heccinavU
kelavE kelavu padagaLondige mAtra baLakeyAguvuvAda kAraNa, avugaLa
svarUpavannu niyamagaLa sahAyadinda varNisuvudu kaSTa. AdarU
kUDa, avugaLa prayOgadalli kelavu 'olavu'gaLannu kANalu sAdhyavide
yAda kAraNa antaha olavugaLannu niyamagaLa rUpadalli varNisuvu
dara mUlaka I pratyayagaLa svarUpada mEle beLakannu cellalu
sAdhyavide.

udAharaNegAgi ike-ige emba pratyaya ellA rItiya kriyApada
gaLondigU baraballudAdare, ta-te emba pratyaya sAmAnyavAgi
ikArAnta mattu ekArAnta kriyApadagaLondige mAtravE bara
balludu; alu emba innondu pratyaya ukArAnta kriyApada
gaLondige mAtravE baraballudu. intaha halavu hELikegaLannu
kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva nAmapadagaLannu pariSIlisuvudara mUlaka
racisi hELalu sAdhyavideyAdarU ivakkella ondalla ondu apavAda


vannu kANalu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa ivu olavugaLallade
niyamagaLalla. padapratyayagaLu I rIti niyamabaddhavAgi
illadiruvudakke avugaLa oLaracanege cAritrika mahatvavideyallade
mAtina baLakeyalli heccina mahatvavillavembudE mukhya kAraNa.

padapratyayagaLa svarUpavEnembudannu varNisuvalli kANisikoLLuva
innondu samasyeyEnendare, sAmAnyavAgi I pratyayagaLu padarUpa
pratyayagaLa hAge ondakkondu sambandhitavAgiruvudilla. udAharaNe
gAgi, padarUpapratyayagaLannu vacanapratyayagaLu, vibhakti pratyayagaLu,
kAlapratyayagaLu, AkhyAtapratyayagaLu ityAdiyAgi bEre bEre gumpu
gaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavide, mattu kelavu sandarbhagaLalli intaha
ondu gumpige sErida padarUpapratyayagaLalli yAvudAdarU ondannu
khaDDAyavAgiyU baLasalEbEkemba niyamavannu mADalu sAdhyavide.
udAharaNegAgi bande embantaha pUrNa kriyArUpagaLalli ghaTaneya
samayavannu sUcisuva kAlapratyayagaLallondannu mattu adara
anantara AkhyAta pratyayagaLallondannu baLasalEbEkemba niyamavide.

padapratyayagaLannu I rIti viSiSTavAda gumpugaLalli vingaDisalu
sAdhyavAguvudilla, mattu avugaLa baLakeyalli khaDDAyavendu hELa
bahudAda niyamagaLU illa. I kAraNakkAgi avugaLannu bariya ondu
paTTiyalli koTTu, ondondAgi avugaLa baLakeyalli kANisuva
olavugaLannaSTE varNisalu sAdhyavAguttade. padapratyayagaLa arthavU
aniyamitavAdudAda kAraNa avannu avu koDuva arthada AdhArada
mElU niyamitavAgi vargIkarisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla.

I pratyayagaLu entaha padagaLondige baruttave, endare nAmapada
gaLondige baruttaveyE, kriyapadagaLondige baruttaveyE athavA
guNapadagaLondige baruttaveyE embudara AdhArada mElU avannu
vyavasthitavAgi vargIkarisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla. avu prAmukhyavAgi
yAva vargada padagaLondige baruttave endaSTE hELalu sAdhyavAgu
ttade. udAharaNegAgi ike-ige emba pratyaya prAmukhyavAgi kriyA
padagaLondige baruvudAdarU (udA: nambike, baLalike, ityAdi),
billugArike, tiLuvaLike modalAda bEre kelavu padagaLalli nAmapada
gaLondigU bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. illU padapratyayagaLa baLake
yalli aniyamitateyE eddu kANisuttade.

I kAraNagaLigAgi, pratyayaviruva padagaLalli kANisuva padapratyaya
gaLannu I keLage bariya paTTiya mUlaka mAtravE vivarisi hELalu


sAdhyavAgide. pratiyondu pratyayada keLagU adara baLakeyalli
kANisuva kelavu olavugaLannu udAharaNegaLa mUlaka vivarisalu
prayatnisa lAgide. I pratyayagaLa sahAyadinda kriyApada illavE
guNapadagaLannu nAmapadagaLannAgi parivartisalAgideyE athavA
nAmapadagaLannE avakkinta bhinnavAda bEre nAmapadagaLannAgi
badalAyisalAgideyE embudannu tiLisuvudakkAgi mAtra I
pratyayagaLannu mUru bEre bEre vibhAgagaLAgi vingaDisalu
prayatnisalAgide. keLage koTTiruva paTTigaLalli yAvudU
sampUrNavAdudalla. I pratyayagaLa svarUpaventahadu embudannu
tiLisalu sahAyakavAguvante jAsti baLakeyalliruva pratyayaviruva
nAmapadagaLalli kANisuva padapratyayagaLannu mAtravE illi
pariSIlisalAgide.

## 4.3 kriyApadagaLinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLu
kannaDada nAmapadagaLalli kANisuva padapratyayagaLalli heccinavU kriyA
padagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguva pratyaya
gaLu. guNapadagaLinda illavE nAmapadagaLinda bEre nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisalu baLasuva padapratyayagaLa sankhye kannaDadalli bahaLa kaDime.
idakkAgi, kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudaralli baLake
yAguva padapratyayagaLannu illi modalige pariSIlisalAgide.

## 4.3.1 ike-ige pratyaya
kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu baLasuva padapratyaya
gaLalli ike-ige mattu ke-ge emba rUpagaLalli baruva pratyayavE
atyanta prAmukhyavAdudu. baLalu-baLalike, oppu-oppige, koDu-
koDuge, hiDi-hiDike modalAda padayugdhagaLalli idu
kriyApadagaLige sErikoLLuvudemba viSaya spaSTavAgiruvudAdarU,
turisu-turike, bayasu-bayake, bEsarisu (bEsara)-bEsarike
modalAdavugaLalli I viSaya aSTondu spaSTavAgilla. bayasu
embudaralli su emba pratyaya mattu bayake embudaralli ke emba
pratyaya yAva vargakkU sErada baya- emba asvatantra padavondakke
sEriveyendu hELalU sAdhyavide. hIgiddarU ike-ige emba I
pratyayavannoLagonDiruva heccina padagaLigU kriyApadavE mUla
embudannu munde nODa liruvevu.


kriyApadagaLinda kriyArUpavondannu paDeyuvudakkAgi baLasuva
ike emba pradarUpa pratyayavondide. idannu baLaluvike, oppuvike,
hiDiyuvike, koDuvike modalAda padarUpagaLalli kANabahudu.
idu rUpadalli mElina pratyayavannE hOluttideyAdarU adakkinta
bhinna vAdudembudannu munde nODaliruvevu.

samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda halavAru padagaLalli ike emba
bErondu pratyaya kANisuttade. udA: pUrva-pUrvika, samAja-
sAmAjika, kSaNa-kSaNika, varSa-vArSika ityAdi. idu sAmAnyavAgi
nAmapadagaLinda nAmaviSESaNagaLannu sAdhisuvalli baLakeyAguttade.
kannaDada ike-ige pratyaya samskxtadinda bandudEnO endu kiTTel
(1894:180,462) avaru sUcisalu I eraDu pratyayagaLa
naDuviruva sArUpya kAraNavirabahudu. Adare iveraDakkU naDuve
halavAru vyatyAsagaLiddu, kannaDa nAmapadagaLa racaneyalli atyanta
prAmukhyavAda sthAnavannu paDediruva ike-ige pratyaya kannaDaddE
endu parigaNisuvudu heccu samanjasavendu tOruttade.

## (ka) rUpabhEdagaLu
I pratyayakke ike, ke, ige mattu ge embudAgi nAlku bEre bEre
rUpagaLive. ivugaLalli ike embudu mukhyavAgi ukAradalli kone
goLLuva kriyApadagaLondige baruttade mattu I pratyaya (hAgU
idara ige emba rUpa) sEridAga kriyApadada koneya ukAra biddu
hOguttade. udA:

baLalu baLalike hELu hELike
bedaru bedarike tOru tOrike
hogaLu hogaLike anju
anjike
agalu agalike nambu nambike

(mUraneya kAlam) embudAgi eraDu vidhadavugaLive. ivugaLalli
eraDakSaradavugaLu modalaneya akSaradalli uddasvaravuLLavugaLu (hELu
mattu tOru) mattu giDDasvaraviddarU sonneyondige baruvavugaLu


(anju mattu nambu) embudAgi eraDu vidhadavugaLembudannu
gamanisabahudu.

ukAradalli konegoLLuva mattu eraDakSaraviruva kriyApadagaLa
modalaneya akSaradalli giDDasvara mAtra ideyAdare athavA giDDasvara
dondige eraDaneya akSaradalli ottakSaravideyAdare, antaha kriyApada
gaLondige I pratyaya ge illavE ige emba rUpadalli baruttade.

kriyApadada koneya ekAra bidduhOgide) mattu naDe-naDuge
embudaralli ekAra ukAravAgide. idallade, I koneya padadalli
keya badalu ge bandide.

rUpadalli baruvudannu suli-sulige mattu holi-holige emba
udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu. Adare hiDi-hiDike embudaralli idu
ke emba rUpadalli bandide. idallade, mEle sUcisidante hiDi
embudu kannaDadalli kriyApadavU havdu, nAmapadavU havdu.

pratyayaviruva padagaLa oLaracaneyalli baLakeyAguva niyamagaLu
olavugaLu mAtra, avugaLige apavAdagaLiruvudu jAsti embudannu I
ike-ige pratyayada baLakeya hindiruva 'niyama'vannu bareyalu
naDesida I prayatna spaSTapaDisuttade. idallade, kannaDada kriyApadagaLalli
yAvavugaLondige I pratyaya baraballudu mattu yAvavugaLondige
baralAradu emba viSayadallU bahaLaSTu aniyamitate ide. udA
haraNegAgi, mADu, kuDi, bare, aDagu, horaDu, kollu, kaTTu,
tumbu, Udu modalAda halavAru kriyApadagaLondige I pratyaya
baLakeyAgilla.

## (kha) arthabhEdagaLu
kriyApadagaLige ike-ige emba pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka
tayArAguva I pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLige artha hELuvudU
bahaLa kaSTavAda kelasavAgide. sAmAnyavAgi I nAmapadagaLu avugaLa
oLaracaneyalli bandiruva kriyApadagaLu yAva ghaTanegaLannu nirdESisu
ttaveyO avannE hesarisuttave. udAharaNegAgi, keLage modalaneya
kAlannalli koTTiruva kriyApadagaLu bEre bEre rItiya ghaTanegaLannu
nirdESisuttiddu, avannE eraDaneya kAlannalli koTTiruva nAmapada
gaLu hesarisuttiveyembudannu gamanisabahudu.

anju anjike
hogaLu hogaLike
bayasu bayake
tUkaDisu tUkaDike

Adare, I niyamakke halavAru bEre bEre rItiya apavAdagaLive.
udAharaNegAgi, moLake, kettige, hAsige, terige modalAdavugaLu
avugaLa oLaracaneyalli baruva moLe, kettu, hAsu, teru modalAda
kriyApadagaLu nirdESisuva ghaTanegaLannu hesarisuva badalu, A ghaTane


gaLinda siddhavAda vastugaLannu hesarisuttave; hiDike, hodike modalA
davugaLu antaha ghaTanegaLannu naDesalu bEkAguva upakaraNagaLannu
hesarisuttave. pratyayaviruva padagaLu 'hesarisuva' padagaLAgiddu, antaha
hesarisuva padagaLa arthavannu avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle
nirdharisuva avaSyakateyillavembudE (3.3.3 nODi) avugaLa artha
dalli intaha aniyamitate kANisikoLLalu mukhya kAraNa.

## (ga) nAmapadadondige baLake
ike-ige pratyayavu adara ike emba rUpadalli nEravAgi kriyApadada
anantara baruva badalu vaLi illavE aLe emba pratyayada anantara
baraballudu, mattu adara ige emba rUpadalli aNe emba pratyayada
anantaravU baraballudu embudannu keLage koTTiruva padagaLalli
kANabahudu.

dara munde ike emba rUpadalli bandide. dabbALike embudaralli I
pratyayadondige ALe emba pratyaya bandiruva hAge kANisuttade.

mEle koTTiruva nAmapadagaLannu kriyApadavondakke eraDu bEre
bEre pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyendu hELuva badalu aLi
illavE aN emba pratyayagaLa baLakeyinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLige
ike-ige pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyendU hELalu sAdhya
vide. huTTuvaLi, sAguvaLi modalAda padagaLalli vaLi emba
pratyayada mUlaka, mattu sAgaNe, tirugaNe modalAda padagaLalli
aNe emba pratyayada mUlaka intaha nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisalAgide.

ondu vyavasAya illavE guNadharmavannAdharisi vyaktigaLannu
hesarisuvantaha (illavE antaha guNadharmavannE sUcisuvantaha)
kelavu SabdagaLige ike emba pratyayavondannu sErisi A vyavasAya
illavE guNadharmavannu hesarisuvantaha nAmapadavannu tayArisalu


sAdhyavide. intaha SabdagaLu nEravAgi samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandu
virabahudu, illavE kannaDada SabdagaLige gAra (illavE vanta) emba
pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisidavugaLirabahudu. udA:

madhyastha madhyasthike billugAra billugArike
SrImanta SrImantike mInugAra mInugArike
unnata unnatike maDivanta
maDivantike

mAsTarik emba padadalli I pratyaya ingliS‌ninda eravalAgi
bandiruva mAsTar emba padadondige bandide.

intaha padagaLalli baruva ike emba pratyaya mEle vivarisiruva
ike-ige pratyayakke sambandhisidudE athavA samskxtadinda eravalAgi
bandiruva bEre kelavu padagaLalli kANisuva ika emba innondu
pratyayakke (udA: kSaNa-kSaNika, yantra-yAntrika ityAdi (vivaragaLige
8.3.5 nODi)) sambandhisidudE emba viSayadalli ondu nirdhArakke
baruvudu svalpa kaSTa.

## (pha) ike emba padarUpa pratyaya
mEle koTTiruva ike-ige emba pratyayadinda bhinnavAgiruva mattu
ellA sandarbhagaLallU ike emba ondE rUpadalliruva padarUpa
pratyayavondu kannaDadalli baLakeyallide. idannu kriyApadagaLige sErisi
avugaLa kriyArUpavondannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. idu kriyApada
gaLu nirdESisuva ghaTanegaLannu varNisuttadallade hesarisuvudilla.
udA:

anju anjuvike bare bareyuvike
mADu mADuvike kuDi kuDiyuvike
hogaLu hogaLuvike iru iruvike
bayasu bayasuvike tappu tappuvike

I pratyayavannu sErisidAga ukArAnta kriyApadagaLa koneyalli
vakAra sErikoLLuttade, mattu ikArAnta mattu ekArAnta kriyApada


gaLa koneyalli vakAra mAtravallade ya emba akSaravU sErikoLLuttade
embudannu mElina udAharaNegaLinda tiLiyabahudu.

ike emba I pratyayavannoLagonDiruva kriyArUpagaLannu nAma
padagaLa sthAnadalli baLasalu sAdhyaviddu, ivakke bEre bEre vibhakti
pratyayagaLannU sErisalu sAdhyavide. udA:

1. (1ka) Akeya hADuvikeyannu ellarU hogaLuttiddAre.
2. (1kha) nimma hogaLuvikeyinda avanu ubbihOgiddAne.
3. (1ga) avaLa aLuvikege kallU karagItu.

1. (i) kelavu vyatyAsagaLu
2. kriyApadagaLinda kriyArUpagaLannu tayArisalu baLasuva I ike emba
3. pratyaya padarUpa pratyayavallade padapratyayavalla. adu mEle
4. vivarisiruva ike-ige emba padapratyayakkinta tIra bhinnavAdudu. pada
5. pratyayagaLigU mattu padarUpa pratyayagaLigU naDuve entaha vyatyAsa
6. gaLella kANisaballuvu embudannu mEle 1.6ralli vivarisalAgide.
7. intaha vyatyAsagaLu I ike-ige mattu ike emba eraDu pratyayagaLa
8. naDuveyU kANisuvuvembudannu avugaLa naDuviruva keLagina vyatyAsa
9. gaLu spaSTapaDisuttave.
10. (1) ike emba padarUpa pratyaya ellA kriyApadagaLondigU
11. baraballudu. I viSayadalli ondU apavAdavilla. samskxtadinda
12. eravalAgi bandiruva mattu isu emba pratyayada mUlaka kannaDadalli
13. kriyApadavAgi baLakeyAguva padagaLondigU idu baraballudembu
14. dannu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu.
16. anumatisu anumatisuvike
17. SikSisu SikSisuvike
18. virOdhisu virOdhisuvike
19. rakSisu rakSisuvike
21. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, ike-ige emba padapratyayada baLake kelavE
22. kelavu kriyApadagaLondige mAtra rUDhiyallide. udAharaNegAgi, bare,
23. kuDi, mADu, duDuku, tirugu modalAda halavAru kriyApada
24. gaLondige I pratyayada baLake rUDhiyallilla. ike emba padarUpa


pratyayavannu ivellavakkU sErisi hELalu sAdhyavide. idallade, samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandiruva anumatisu, SikSisu modalAda kriyApada
gaLondige ike emba padarUpa pratyayavannu sErisi hELuva hAge
ike-ige emba padapratyayavannu sErisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.

(2) ike emba padarUpa pratyayada baLakeyalli ike-ige emba
padapratyayada baLakeyalli kANisuvantaha aniyamita badalAvaNega
LAvuvU kANisuvudilla. ellA rItiya kriyApadagaLondigU adu
ike emba ondE rUpadalli baruttade. mEle sUcisidante, ukArada
anantara vakAra sErikoLLuvudu mattu ekAra hAgU ikAragaLa
anantara yav embudu sErikoLLuvudu emba eraDu sandhiniyama
gaLu mAtra ivugaLa baLakeyalli kANisuva badalAvaNegaLu. I eraDu
badalAvaNegaLu ellA sandarbhagaLallU niyamitavAgi baruttiddu, avakke
yAva apavAdavU illa.

kriyApadagaLU kUDa, ike emba padarUpa pratyayadondige
svalpavU badalAvaNeyillade sErikoLLuttave. udAharaNegAgi, kriyApada
gaLa koneyalli baruva su emba pratyaya illavE u emba svara I
pratyaya sEridAga biddu hOguvudilla, mattu kriyApadagaLa kone
yalli baruva ekAra akAravAgi illavE ukAravAgi badalAguvudilla.
ike-ige emba padapratyayakkU mattu ike emba padarUpa pratyayakkU
naDuviruva I vyatyAsavannu keLage koTTiruva udAharaNegaLalli kANa
bahudu.

(3) arthada maTTigU I eraDu pratyayagaLa naDuve vyatyAsavide.
mEleyE vivarisidante, ike-ige pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida
nAmapadagaLige avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle niyamitavAgi
artha hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. avellavakkU oLaracane ondE rItiya
dAdarU artha mAtra aniyamitavAgi bEre bErAgiruttade. Adare,
ike emba padarUpa pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida ellA kriyArUpa
gaLigU ondE rItiya arthavide. avella varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka
avugaLalli bandiruva kriyApadavu nirdESisuva ghaTaneyannu gurutisu
ttave.

bayasu bayake bayasuvike

kettu kettige kettuvike

hAsu hAsuge hAsuvike

hiDi hiDike hiDiyuvike

moLe moLake moLeyuvike

holi holige holiyuvike

I ellA vyatyAsagaLa AdhArada mEle ike embudu kriyA
padagaLinda kriyArUpagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva padarUpa
pratyayavendU mattu ike-ige embudu prAmukhyavAgi kriyApada
gaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva adakkinta tIra
bhinnavAda padapratyayavendU hELabEkAguttade.

## 4.3.2 ta-tE pratyaya
ikAra mattu ekAragaLalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLige ta illavE te
emba rUpadalliruva I pratyayavannu sErisi kelavu nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisalu sAdhyavide. I eraDu rUpagaLalli te embudara baLake
gintalU ta embudara baLakeyE jAsti. Adare ivugaLalli yAvudannu
elli baLasabEku emba viSayadalli niyamavEnU iruva hAge
kANisuvudilla. te embudarondige bandAga kriyApadagaLa koneya
ekAra akAravAguttade (udA: naDe-naDate), Adare ta embuda
rondige bandAga adu hAgeyE badalAgade uLiyuttade (udA:
hoDe-hoDeta).


I pratyayada mUlaka tayArAda nAmapadagaLu sAmAnyavAgi
kriyApadavu nirdESisuva ghaTaneyannu illavE adarinda siddhavAguva
guNadharmavannu hesarisuttave. udA:

aniyamitavAgi intaha nAmapadagaLu kriyApadavu nirdESisuva
ghaTaneyalli baruva vastu, prANi modalAduvannu hesarisuttiralU
sAdhyavide (udA: miDi-miDite). tappu-tappita embudaralli I
pratyaya ukAradalli konegoLLuva kriyApadadondigU bandiruva hAge
kANisuttade.

samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva kelavu nAmapadagaLalli te
emba pratyayavondu kANisuttade. udA:

adhyakSa adhyakSate
arha arhate
kavi kavite
dakSa dakSate

Adare I te emba pratyayavannu nAmapadagaLigallade kriyApadagaLige
sErisuvudilla. vyaktiyobbanannu hesarisuva nAmapadadinda A vyaktiya
guNadharmavannu hesarisuva bErondu nAmapadavannu sAdhisalu I
pratyayada baLakeyAguttade. idu samskxtada tA emba pratyayada kannaDa
rUpa. mEle vivarisiruva ta-te idakkinta bhinnavAdudu.


## 4.3.3 A pratyaya
idu mukhyavAgi gu illavE Du emba akSaragaLalli konegoLLuva
kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvalli baLakeyAguttade. I
pratyaya sEridAga kriyApadagaLa koneyalliruva gu mattu Du emba
akSaragaLu k mattu T endAguttave (endare, gakAra, DakAragaLu
kakAra, TakAragaLAguttave mattu avugaLa anantara baruva ukAra
bidduhOguttade).

<td>tUka</td>

<td>kATa</td>

ADu embudaralli konegoLLuva halavu 'kUDu'kriyApadagaLu
kannaDadalliddu avugaLalli kelavu kriyApadagaLondige I pratyaya bara
balludu. intaha baLakeyallU kriyApadada koneya Du emba akSara
T endAguttade. udA:

hOrADu hOrATa

tirugADu tirugATa

ODADu ODATa

baddADu baddATa

Adare I pratyaya intaha ellA kUDukriyApadagagaLondigU
niyamitavAgi baruvudilla. udAharaNegAgi, bisADu, nagADu, mAta
nADu modalAdavugaLondige idu baruvudilla, mattu I pratyayava
nnoLagonDiruva mArATa, huDugATa modalAda bEre kelavu
nAmapadagaLige samanAda kUDukriyApada kannaDadalli baLakeyallilla.
idallade, taletiruka, dArihOka modalAda bEre kelavu nAmapada
gaLalli I pratyaya bandiruva hAge kANisuttade, Adare ivannu
tayArisalu bEkAguva kUDukriyApadagaLu kannaDadalli baLakeyallilla.


Udu emba kriyApadakke idE pratyayavannu sErisi Uta emba
padavannu tayArisiruvalli dakAra takAravAgiruvudannu kANabahudu.

I pratyayada mUlaka tayArAguva nAmapadagaLa arthavU
aniyamitavAdudu. heccineDegaLallU idu kriyApadavu nirdESisuva
ghaTaneyannu hesarisuttade (udA: naDugu-naDuka, marugu-maruka).
Adare, kelaveDegaLalli ondu viSiSTavAda ghaTaneyannu mAtravE hesarisu
ttade (udA: mADu-mATa), mattu bEre kelavu kaDegaLalli antaha
ghaTaneyannu naDesuva vyaktiyannu hesarisuttade (udA: tirugu-tiruka).

agalu-agali mattu tIru-tIra embavugaLalli idE pratyaya ru
mattu lu emba akSaragaLalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLondige
bandiruvudannu kANabahudu.

## 4.3.5 vaLi pratyaya
kriyApadagaLige I pratyayavannu sErisidAga, avugaLa koneyalli baruva
ekAra akAravAguttade, mattu ikAra ukAravAguttade. Adare ukAra
mAtra badalAgade hAgeyE uLiyuttade. idallade, udA:

<table>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>hiDi</td>
<td>hiDuvaLi</td>

tiLuvaLike mattu naDavaLike emba eraDu padagaLalli I pratyaya ke
emba innondu pratyayadondige bandide. mattu ADaLita emba
padadalli ta emba pratyayadondige bandide. idallade, ADaLita emba


padadalli kriyApadadallidda LakAra DakAravAgide, mattu vaLi pratyayada
vakAra biddu hOgide.

gottu emba AkhyAta padadondigU I pratyaya bandiruvudannu
gottuvaLi emba nAmapadadalli kANabahudu. dabbALike
embudarallU idE pratyaya (dabbu emba kriyApadadondige)
bandiralu sAdhyaviddu, illi idakke ALi emba rUpavide.

aLi emba rUpadalliruva pratyayavondu AkaLisu, appaLisu,
kuppaLisu, bikkaLisu modalAda kelavu kriyApadagaLalli baruvudembu
dannu munde AranE adhyAyadalli nODaliruvevu. adu I pratyayakke
sambandhisiralu sAdhyavide. idE pratyaya heggaLike emba padadalli hiri
emba guNapadada heg emba rUpadondige bandide.

## 4.3.6 vaN pratyaya

koneya ekAra I pratyaya sEridAga akAravAguttade mattu ukAra
biddu hOguttade. ukAradalli konegoLLuva kriyApadadondige idu
aN emba rUpadalli baruttade.

## 4.3.10 'sonne' pratyaya
kannaDadalli kelavu padagaLannu avugaLalli yAva badalAvaNeyannU
mADade nAmapadagaLannAgi illavE kriyApadagaLannAgi baLasalu sAdhya
vide. udAharaNegAgi, keLage koTTiruva (2ka-ga) vAkyagaLannu gamanisa
bahudu.

1. (2ka) avaLu ondu hADannu hADidaLu.
2. (2kha) guDugu guDugitu, mincu mincitu.
3. (2ga) avanu kaTTida kaTTu saDilAgide.

(2ka)dalli hADu emba pada eraDu bAri bandiddu, modalaneya baLake
yalli adu nAmapadavAgiyU mattu eraDaneya baLakeyalli kriyApada
vAgiyU bandide. idE rItiyalli (2kha)dalli guDugu mattu
mincu emba padagaLu mattu (2ga)dalli kaTTu emba pada yAva
rItiya badalAvaNegU oLagAgade nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLAgi
bandiru vudannu kANabahudu.

intaha padagaLu mUladalli kriyApadagaLendU, mattu
avakkondu 'sonne' pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka avugaLinda
nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalAgideyendU hELuva kramavide. kannaDadalli


sAmAnyavAgi kriyApadagaLinda pratyayagaLannu sErisi nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisuvudE jAsti. isu emba pratyayavannu baLasi nAmapadagaLinda
kriyApadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavideyEnO nija. Adare idakke
kannaDada nAmapada gaLigintalU samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda
nAmapadagaLannu baLasu vudE jAsti (6.4 nODi). idakkinta bhinnavAda
pratyayagaLu kannaDada kriyApadagaLalli cAritrika avaSESagaLAgi mAtra
kANisikoLLuttave (6.3 nODi).

I viSayagaLa AdhArada mEle, nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLa
naDuve sambandhaviruvallella kriyApadavE mUlavendU mattu nAma
pada kriyApadakke yAvudAdarondu pratyayavannu (illavE padavannu)
sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAguvantahadendU vAdisalu sAdhyavide.

I rIti nAmapadagaLigU mattu kriyApadagaLigU ondE rUpa
viruvudannu I keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu.

<td>guDugu</td>

</tr>

<td>uri</td>
<td>tappu</td>
<td>baduku</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>beLe</td>
<td>kaTTu</td>
<td>uguLu</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>kare</td>
<td>guddu</td>
<td>uruLu</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

intaha padagaLa prayOgadalli kriyApadagaLu niyamitavAgi ondu
ghaTaneyannu nirdESisuvuvAdare, nAmapadagaLu aniyamitavAgi bEre
bEre rItiya arthagaLannu koDuttave. udAharaNegAgi, Odu, aLu,
kemmu modalAda nAmapadagaLu adE rUpada kriyApadagaLu nirdE
Sisuva ghaTanegaLannu hesarisuvuvAdare, hADu, beLe, bevaru
modalAda nAmapadagaLu antaha ghaTanegaLinda doreyuva
phalitAmSavannu hesarisu ttave.

arthadalli aniyamitate mattu vayvidhyavannu nAvu sAmAnyavAgi
pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLallE kANuvevAda kAraNa, intaha nAmapada
gaLalli kriyApadagaLondige ondu 'sonne' pratyaya bandideyemba
mElina vAdakke I nAmapadagaLa arthadalli kANisuva aniyamitate
yU ondu AdhAravAgaballudu.


## 4.3.11 bEre kelavu pratyayagaLu
mEle vivarisiruva pratyayagaLu mAtravallade, onderaDu padagaLalli
mAtravE kANisikoLLuva bEreyU kelavu pratyayagaLu kannaDadalli
kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave.
ivannu bEre bErAgi varNisuva badalu paTTimADi hELuvudE sulabha
vAdudarinda antaha pratyayagaLiruva padagaLa paTTiyondannu keLage
koDalAgide.

## 4.4 nAmapadagaLinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLu
kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLannu bEre nAmapadagaLige yAvudAdarondu
pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlakavU tayArisalu sAdhyavide. udA
haraNegAgi, gANiga emba nAmapadavannu gANa emba bErondu nAma
padakke iga pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgide mattu mUguti emba
nAmapadavannu mUru emba bErondu nAmapadakke ti emba
pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgide.

Adare kannaDadalli I rIti tayArisalAgiruva nAmapadagaLa sankhye
jAsti illa. sAmAnyavAgi nAmapadagaLannu bEre nAmapadagaLondige
illavE kriyApada athavA guNapadagaLondige sErisi jODupadagaLannu
tayArisuvudE kannaDadalli heccu baLakeyalliruva vidhAna. udAharaNe
gAgi, kay emba nAmapadavannu baLasi halavu oLaracaneyiruva nAma
padagaLannu tayArisalAgiddu, ivellavU jODupadagaLa rUpadalliruvu
dannu gamanisabahudu.

kaykoDali kaygUsu
kaygannaDi kaycIla
kaygADi kaycaLaka
kaygelasa kaypiDi
kaygUli kaybaraha
kaygaDa kaymagga, ityAdi


nAmapadagaLinda bEre nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva
pratyayagaLu kelavu kannaDadalli kANisuvuvAdarU, avugaLalli samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandavugaLu illavE samskxtada pratyayagaLa mAdari
yalli siddhavAdavugaLE jAsti. udAharaNegAgi, samskxtada kx 'mADu'
emba kriyApadadinda siddhavAda kAra emba pratyaya (udA: citrakAra,
namaskAra, balAtkAra ityAdi) kannaDadalli gAra emba pratyayavAgi
halavu nAmapadagaLalli kANisikoLLuttade. udA:

idE rItiyalli, mEle 4.3.1ralli vivarisida hAge, samskxtada
ike emba pratyayada mAdariyalli ondu vyavasAya illavE
guNadharma vannAdharisi vyaktigaLannu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLinda A
vyavasAya illavE guNadharmavannu hesarisuva nAmapadavannu
tayArisalu kannaDadalli ike emba pratyayada baLakeyAguttade.
kolegArike, billugArike, modalAda nAmapadagaLannu idakke
udAharaNegaLannAgi koDabahudu.

kannaDadavE Ada kelavu padagaLalli kANisuva strI-puruSa lingabhEda
vannu sUcisuva i mattu a emberaDu pratyayagaLigU (udA:
muduka-muduki) samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva bEre
halavu padagaLalli kANisuva idE rUpada pratyayagaLu (udA: naTa-
naTi, lEkhaka-lEkhaki, SikSaka-SikSaki, ityAdi) mAdariyAgiralu sAdhya
vide. Adare, ukAradalli konegoLLuva halavu guNapadagaLindalU
vyavasthitavAgi I pratyayagaLannu baLasi nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu
sAdhya embudannu munde 4.5ralli nODaliruvevu.

ganDu-heNNu emba arthabhEdavannu sUcisuva bEreyU kelavu
pratyayagaLu kannaDadallive. udAharaNegAgi, mEle koTTiruva gAra


emba pratyayadalli konegoLLuva nAmapadagaLalli kelavakke ti emba
pratyayavannu sErisi heNNu emba artha baruvante mADalu sAdhyavide.
udA:

baLegAra baLegArti
mAlegAra mAlegArti
edegAra edegArti
jotegAra jotegArti

vastu, viSaya, sthaLa modalAduvannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLige
iga pratyayavannu sErisi, A vastu, viSaya, sthaLa modalAduvakke
sambandhisiruva vyaktigaLannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu
sAdhyavide. udA:
