## 5.8 kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva vibhajanegaLu
kannaDada heccina vyAkaraNagaLallU 'samAsagaLu' emba ondu adhyAya
viddu, adaralli kannaDada jODupadagaLa vibhajane mattu varNane
yiruttade. Adare I vibhajane heccina maTTige samskxta vayyAkaraNigaLu
A bhASeyalli baruva jODupadagaLa vibhajanegAgi baLasida vidhAnavannE
avalambiside. samskxtada samAsagaLu yAvuvu, avugaLalli yAvuvu
kannaDadallU kANisuttave, mattu samskxtadallilladantaha bEre yAva
samAsagaLu kannaDadallive embantaha praSnegaLige uttaravannu huDukutta
I vibhajane sAguttade.

Adare I rIti samskxta samAsagaLa dxSTikOnada mUlaka kannaDada
jODupadagaLannu varNisuvudarindAgi A varNane anavaSyakavAgi bahaLa
kliSTavAguttade mAtravalla, nijakkU kannaDada jODupadagaLu yAva
rIti yavu emba praSnege nEravAda uttara siguvudE illa. mEle
(5.6ralli) I toDaku toDakAda vidhAnavannu toredu, kannaDadalli
baLakeyalliruva jODupadagaLannu nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneyalli
kANisuva vaySiSTya gaLa AdhArada mEle vibhajisi vivarisalAgide.

I rIti kannaDada jODupadagaLa nEravAda pariSIlaneyinda sidda
vAda vibhajane ivattina kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva vibhajaneginta
yAva rItiyalli bhinnavAgide embudannu svalpa skUlavAgiyAdarU pari
SIlisuvudu avaSya. yAkendare, hAge mADuvudarinda I kannaDa
vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva vibhajanegaLu yAva rItiyallella asamarpaka
vAgive emba viSaya spaSTavAdItu.

tatpuruSa, karmadhAraya, dvigu, bahuvrIhi, dvandva mattu
avyayibhAvagaLemba Aru samskxta samAsagaLannU mattu ivakkinta
bhinnavAda kriyAsamAsa mattu gamakasamAsagaLemba bEre eraDu
rItiya samAsagaLannU tOrisuva jODupadagaLu kannaDadalliveyembu
dAgi hadimUraneya SatamAnada SabdamaNidarpaNavemba vyAkaraNadalli
hELalAgide. idu haLegannaDadalli baruva jODupadagaLa vibhajane


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


yAgideyAdarU hosagannaDakkU idannE anvayisi hELuvudu rUDhi.
ivattina kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli heccinavugaLallU I vibhajaneyannE
alpasvalpa vyatyAsagaLannu mADi hosagannaDaddendu hELiruvudannu kANa
bahudu.

## 5.8.1 vibhajaneya AdhAra
I vibhajanege AdhAravAgi jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva
padagaLa varga, avugaLa naDuviruva sambandha, mattu jODupadagaLalli
kEndra binduvina sthAna emba I mUru viSayagaLannU oTTAgi
baLasikoLLa lAgide. udAharaNegAgi, jODupadada modalaneya anga
sankhyA vAcakavAgiddare adannu dviguvendU, mattu eraDaneyadu
kriyApada vAgiddare adannu kriyAsamAsavendU kareyalAguttade.
idu jODu padagaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva padagaLa vargavannAdharisida
vibhajane.

jODupadada angagaLeraDu nAmapadagaLAgiddu bEre bEre vibhakti
gaLalliddare adannu tatpuruSavendu kareyalAguttade, mattu ondE
vibhaktiyalliddare adannu karmadhArayavendu kareyalAguttade. idu
jODupadada angagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannAdharisida vibhajane.

jODupadada kEndra bindu eraDaneya angada mEliddare adannu
tatpuruSavendU, modalaneya angada mEliddare avyayibhAva
(illavE amSi samAsa) endU, eraDara mElU iddare dvandva
vendU mattu kEndra bindu jODupadada yAva angada mElU
bILade adara horagiruva ondu padada mEle biddideyAdare adannu
bahuvrIhiyendU kareyalAguttade. idu jODupadadalli kEndra
binduvina sthAnavannAdharisida vibhajane. (jODupadada kEndra bindu
vinalliruva padavannu kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli 'pradhAna pada' embudAgi
kareyuvudu rUDhi).

kannaDada jODupadagaLa vibhajaneyannu I rIti mUru bEre bEre
viSayagaLannu oTTige AdhAravAgi irisikoDu tayArisiruva kAraNa
anavaSyakavAgi gondalakkeDeyAgide. udAharaNegAgi, kEndra bindu
eraDaneya angada mEliruva karmadhAraya, dvigu, kriyAsamAsa
mattu gamakasamAsagaLu tatpuruSada prabhEdagaLendu hELabEkAgu
ide, mattu angagaLeraDU ondE vibhaktiyalli baruva dvigusamAsa
vembudu karmadhArayada prabhEdavendu hELabEkAguttade. yAvu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


dAdarondu sankhye modalaneya angavAgi bandiruva jODupada
dviguvAgiralU sAdhyavide, gamakavAgiralU sAdhyavide; hAgAgi, nijakkU
averaDara naDuvina vyatyAsavEnu, gamakavemba samAsa vidhAna kannaDakke
avaSyavE endella vAda vivAdagaLu idarindAgi mUDi bandive.

idallade, kEndra binduvina sthAnavannAdharisida vibhajane kannaDada
maTTige aSTondu upayuktavAdudalla. yAkendare, kannaDada heccina
jODupadagaLallU eraDaneya anga nAmapadavAgiddu, kEndra bindu
A eraDaneya padada mEleyE bILuttade. kelavu jODupadagaLalli
(prAmukhyavAgi guNapadagaLiruvavugaLalli) mAtra kEndra bindu adara
horagiralu sAdhya (5.6.4 nODi). Adare samskxtada jODupada
gaLannu vibhajisuvalli kEndra binduvina sthAnavemba I viSaya prAmukhya
vAda pAtravannu vahisuttade. I kAraNakkAgiyU samskxtada samAsa
gaLannu alpasvalpa badalAvaNegaLa mUlaka kannaDakke aLavaDisuva prayatna
dindAgi gondalavunTAgide.

jODupadagaLa vibhajanege AdhAravAgaballa bEre bEre viSaya
gaLannu I rIti oTTu sErisalu yatnisade avannu bEre bErAgi irisi
konDu, avu jODupadagaLa vibhajanege yAva rItiyallella sahAyaka
vAgaballuvu embudannu pariSIlisi, anantara avugaLalli atyanta heccu
sahAyakavAgaballa viSayavannu vibhajanege AdhAravAgi tegedukoLLu
vudE sariyAda dAri. kannaDada maTTige mEle (5.6.4ralli) vivarisi
dante, jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva padagaLa vargavannAdharisida
vibhajaneyE atyanta upayuktavAda vibhajane.

## 5.8.2 padavargagaLa sankhye
kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva jODupadagaLa vibhajanegaLu padavarga
gaLa viSayadalli kannaDakkU mattu samskxtakkU naDuviruva prAmukhya
vAda ondu vyatyAsavannu sariyAgi gamanisadiruvudarindAgi bahaLa
maTTige tappu hAdi hiDidive. samskxtadalli nAmapada mattu kriyApada
gaLemba eraDE eraDu mukhya padavargagaLiddu, guNapadagaLa artha
koDuva padagaLalli heccinavU nAmapadavemba padavargadallEnE sEri
koLLuttave.

idakke vyatiriktavAgi kannaDadalli nAmapada, kriyApada mattu
guNapadagaLemba mUru bEre bEre mukhya padavargagaLive embudannu
nAvu mEle eraDaneya adhyAyadalli (2.2ralli) nODiruvevu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


guNapadagaLa artha koDuva nAmapadagaLannu innondu nAmapada
dondige sErisi padagucchavondannu tayArisabEkiddalli, adakke A nAma
padada linga-vacana-vibhaktigaLannu sUcisuva pratyayavannu sErisikoLLa
bEku embudu samskxtada vAkyaracaneya ondu niyama. udAharaNe
gAgi, I keLagina samskxta vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu.

1. (9ka) tatra EkaH kxSNaH sarpaH asti.
2. alli ondu kappu hAvu ide.
4. (10ka) hariH Ekam kxSNam sarpam apaSyat.
5. hari ondu kappu hAvannu nODida.
7. (11ka) hariH EkEna kxSNEna sarpENa daSTaH.
8. hari ondu kappu hAvininda kaccalpaTTa.

mEle koTTiruva (9ka) vAkyadalli EkaH kxSNaH sarpaH 'ondu kappu
hAvu' emba nAmapadaguccha bandiddu, adaralliruva mUru padagaLU
pullinga-Ekavacana-prathamAvibhakti pratyayadondige bandive.

idE nAmapadaguccha (10ka) mattu (11ka) vAkyagaLallU bandiddu,
adaralliruva mUru padagaLU (10ka) vAkyadalli pullinga-Ekavacana-
dvitIyAvibhakti pratyayadondigU (Ekam kxSNam sarpam embudAgi),
mattu (11ka) vAkyadalli pullinga-Ekavacana-txtIyA vibhakti pratyaya
dondigU (EkEna kxSNEna sarpENa embudAgi) bandive.

illi mukhyavAgi gamanisabEkAda viSayavEnendare, I padagucchada
mUraneya angavAda sarpaH 'hAvu' emba pada mAtravallade adara
modalaneya angavAda EkaH 'ondu' emba pada mattu eraDaneya
angavAda kxSNaH 'kappu' emba pada - iveraDU I rIti linga-
vacana-vibhakti pratyayadondige barabEkAgide. idu samskxtadalli
padagucchagaLannu tayArisuva ondu niyama.

kannaDa padagucchagaLa racane idakkinta tIra bhinnavAdudu. avugaLalli
baruva padagaLalli koneyadakke mAtra vibhakti pratyayagaLannu mattu
vacana pratyayagaLannu sErisalu sAdhyavide. mEle koTTiruva samskxta
vAkyagaLa kannaDa anuvAdagaLannu gamanisidevAdare I viSaya
spaSTavAdItu. EkaH kxSNaH sarpaH emba samskxta padagucchada


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


modalaneya padada kannaDa anuvAda ondu embudu. I pada mEle
koTTiruva mUru vAkya gaLallU ondE rUpadalli bandiruvudannu
gamanisabahudu.

idE rItiyalli adE padagucchada eraDaneya padada anuvAdavAda
vAgiruva kappu emba padavU kannaDada I mUru vAkyagaLallU ondE
rUpadalli bandide. annu mattu inda emba vibhakti pratyayagaLannu
(10ka) mattu (11ka) vAkyagaLalli I padagucchada mUraneya padavAda
hAvu embudakke mAtravE sErisalAgideyallade, samskxtadalliruva
hAge modalaneya mattu eraDaneya padagaLige sErisilla embudannu
gamanisabahudu.

kannaDadalli guNapadagaLu nAmapadagaLiginta bhinnavAda bEreyE
ondu padavargadalli baruttave mattu nAmapadagaLondige avannu
nEravAgi (vibhakti pratyayagaLa sahAyavillade) baLasalu sAdhya emba
kannaDa vAkyaracaneya niyama mEle koTTiruva samskxta vAkyaracaneya
niyamakkinta bhinnavAgiruvudE I vyatyAsakke kAraNa.

samskxtadalli EkaH kxSNaH sarpaH emba padagucchada badalu EkaH
kxSNasarpaH embudAgi adaralliruva eraDaneya mattu mUraneya pada
gaLannu oTTu sErisi ondu jODupadavannAgi mADi baLasalu sAdhya
vide. intaha jODupadadalli modalaneya angavAgi baruva pada tanna
linga-vacana-vibhakti pratyayavannu kaLedukoLLuttade embudu samskxtada
ondu padaracaneya niyama. I kAraNakkAgi, kxSNaH emba padavannu
ondu jODupadada angavAgi baLasidAga adu ellA rItiya
vAkyagaLallU ondE rUpadalli baruttade. idannu keLage koTTiruva (kha)
vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.

1. (9kha) tatra EkaH kxSNasarpaH asti.
2. alli ondu kappu hAvu ide.
4. (10kha) hariH Ekam kxSNasarpam apaSyat.
5. hari ondu kappu hAvannu nODida.
7. (11kha) hariH EkEna kxSNasarpENa daSTaH.
8. hari ondu kappu hAvininda kaccalpaTTa.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


mElina kannaDa vAkyagaLalli bandiruva kappu hAvu emba padaguccha
samskxtada I kxSNasarpaH emba jODupadavannu hOluvudAda
kAraNa (eraDarallU modalina angavAgi baruva padadondige vibhakti
pratyaya bandillavAda kAraNa) adU karmadhArayavemba samAsadinda
tayArAda jODupadavembudAgi kannaDa vayyAkaraNigaLellarU tappAgi
grahisikonDiddAre. nijakkU kappu hAvu embudu kannaDada vAkya
racaneya niyamagaLa prakAra tayArAda padagucchavallade jODupada
valla. jODupadagaLalli kANisuva guNadharmagaLAvuvU adaralli kANi
suvudilla.

idE rItiyalli nAmapadadondige guNapadavondannu sErisi
tayArisida doDDa mane, cikka pustaka, kempu SAyi, biLi kAgada
modalAdavugaLalli modalaneya angavAgi bandiruva pada vibhakti
pratyayadondige bandillavAdarU kannaDadalli jODupadagaLalla, bariya
padagucchagaLu.

illi gamanisabEkAgiruva viSayavEnendare, angagaLAgi baruva
eraDu padagaLannu vibhakti pratyayavondu pratyEkisuttadeyE athavA
illavE emba viSayada AdhArada mEle samskxtadalli padagucchagaLannu
jODupadagaLinda bErpaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide, Adare kannaDadalli idu
sAdhyavilla.

## 5.8.3 viSESaNagaLu mattu viSESyagaLu
samskxtadalli nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLemba eraDu bEre bEre
padavargagaLige sEruva padagaLillavAda kAraNa, adara padagucchagaLalli
baruva padagaLoLage viSESaNa-viSESya sambandhavannu kalpisuvudu bahaLa
kaSTa. udAharaNegAgi mEle koTTiruva kxSNaH sarpaH emba padaguccha
dalli yAvudu viSESaNa mattu yAvudu viSESya embudannu niSkxSTa
vAgi tiLisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.

padagucchagaLa modalaneya sthAnadalli baruva pada viSESaNavendu
hELuvudAdare, sarpaH kxSNaH embudAgi A padagucchadalliruva padagaLa
sthAnavannu badalisi hELalu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, sarpaH emba
padavU modalaneya sthAnakke bandu viSESaNavendenisaballudu. I
kAraNakkAgi, yAvudu viSESaNa mattu yAvudu viSESya embudu
intaha padagucchagaLannu baLasuvavara dxSTikOnavannavalambisideyallade
avugaLalli angagaLAgi baruva padagaLa svarUpa illavE guNadharma


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


vannavalambisilla embudAgi patanjaliyantaha samskxta vayyAkaraNigaLu
abhiprAyapaTTiddAre.

kannaDada padagucchagaLu idakkinta tIra bhinnavAdavugaLu. kannaDada
kappu hAvu emba padagucchadalli kappu embudu viSESaNavAgi
mAtravE nillaballudu mattu hAvu embudu viSESavAgi mAtravE
nillaballudu. adaralliruva padagaLa sthAnavannu badalAyisi hAvu kappu
endu hELidevAdare adu samskxtadalliruvante ondu padagucchavAgi
uLiyade ondu vAkyavAgibiDuttade.

kannaDadalli modalaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruva kaydIpa, tAyi
mane modalAda jODupadagaLigU mattu modalaneya anga guNa
padavAgiruva doDDamma, beNkallu modalAda jODupadagaLigU
naDuve spaSTavAda vyatyAsagaLive. Adare samskxtada jODupadagaLalli
intaha vyatyAsavannu kANalu sAdhyavAgadu. hAgAgi, guNadharmavannu
sUcisuva padavondannu baLasi racisida kxSNasarpaH embantaha jODu
padagaLannu mAtravallade vastuvannu sUcisuva padavondannu baLasi
racisida candramukham, gOgarbhiNI embantaha jODupadagaLannU
samskxtada vayyAkaraNigaLu karmadhArayavendu parigaNisabEkAgide.

nijakkU kxSNaH emba pada samskxtadalli kannaDada kappu emba padada
hAge ondu guNadharmavannu sUcisuvudilla. idakke badalu A
guNadharmavannu paDediruva obba vyakti illavE ondu vastuvannu adu
sUcisuttade (2.2 nODi). hAgAgi, samskxtadalli eraDu nAmapadagaLa
sErikeyinda tayArAda tatpuruSakkU mattu I karmadhArayakkU
naDuviruva vyatyAsa avugaLa angagaLAgi baruva padagaLu oLanuDiyalli
(vigrahavAkyadalli) yAva vibhaktiya mUlaka sambandhitavAguttave
embudu mAtra. avu prathamA vibhaktiya mUlaka sambandhitavAguvu
vAdare karmadhArayavenisuttave mattu itara vibhaktigaLa mUlaka
sambandhitavAguvuvAdare tatpuruSavenisuttave.

kannaDakkU mattu samskxtakkU naDuve intaha joDupadagaLa racane
yalli bahaLa mukhyavAda vyatyAsagaLiveyAda kAraNa, kannaDada jODu
padagaLu samskxtada jODupadagaLa hAgeyE embudAgi bhramisi
avannu vivarisalu yatnisidalli, mattu avannu samskxtada tatpuruSa,
karmadhAraya mattu dvigugaLemba samAsagaLemba hesarugaLannu baLasi
vingaDisalu yatnisidalli anavaSyakavAgi gondalavunTAgadiradu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


## 5.8.4 subanta pratyaya
samskxtada nAmapadagaLu manuSyarannu gurutisuttirali, illavE bEre
prANi, mara-giDa, vastu, viSaya modalAduvannu gurutisuttirali,
avugaLa lingavembudu A padagaLa koneya akSaraventahadu mattu
avugaLondige baruva vibhakti pratyayagaLige entaha rUpavide emba
viSayada mEle avalambiside. A padagaLa arthavEnu embudu illi
prAmukhyavAda viSayavalla. keLage koTTiruva samskxtada pullinga,
strIlinga mattu napumsaka lingada padagaLannu pariSIlisidalli I viSaya
spaSTavAdItu.

pullinga strIlinga napumsaka linga
nxpaH 'arasu' jananI 'tAyi' jYAnam 'tiLuvaLike'
vxkSaH 'mara' mAlA 'mAle' udakam 'nIru'
aSvaH 'kudure' AjYA 'AjYe' brahma 'paramAtma'
anilaH 'gALi' dhanU 'billu' kalatram 'henDati'
dArAH 'henDati' patni 'henDati' puram 'paTTaNa'

ivugaLalli dArAH ‘henDati’ emba pada bahuvacanadalli mAtra
baruttade.

samskxtada innondu vaySiSTyavEnendare, adaralli linga, vacana
mattu vibhaktigaLannu sUcisalu kannaDadalliruva hAge bEre bEre pratyaya
gaLilla. ivu mUrannU padada koneyalli baruva subanta emba
hesarina ondE pratyaya sUcisuttade. udAharaNegAgi mEle koTTiruva
padagaLellavU (dArAH embudannu biTTu) alli sUcisiruva lingavannu
mAtravallade Ekavacana mattu prathamA vibhaktigaLannU sUcisuva pratyaya
vondarondige bandive.

kannaDada nAmapadagaLa linga bhEda I rIti koneya akSaravannu
illavE vibhakti pratyayada rUpavannu avalambisirade avu gurutisuva
vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa svarUpavannavalambiside. sAmAnyavAgi
ganDasarannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLu pullingadallU, hengasarannu
gurutisuva nAmapadagaLu strIlingadallU mattu uLida nAmapadagaLu
napumsaka lingadallU baruttaveyendu kannaDadalli ondu niyamavannu
mADalu sAdhyavide. idakke kelavE kelavu apavAdagaLu mAtra ive.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


I kAraNakkAgi, kannaDada arthakOSagaLalli nAmapadagaLa linga
yAvudu embudannu sUcisuva avaSyakateyilla. Adare samskxtada
arthakOSadalli pratiyondu nAmapadadeduru adara linga yAvudu
embudannu sUcisuvudu atyavaSya.

kannaDadalli bahuvrIhi emba hesarina samAsavideyE athavA
illavE, mattu ideyAdare adakke kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLu koDuva cala
vAdi, haNegaNNa, geDDemUga modalAda jODupadagaLu udAharaNe
gaLAgaballuvE embudannu tiLiyalu kannaDakkU mattu samskxtakkU
naDuve linga-vacana-vibhakti pratyayagaLa prayOgadalli kANisuva I
vyatyAsavannu gamanadallirisikoLLuvudu avaSya. ondu jODupadada
kEndra bindu A padada angagaLAgiruva padagaLa mEle bILade
horagiruva padavondara mEle biddideyAdare (endare horagiruva
pada 'pradhAna pada'vAgideyAdare), antaha padada tayArikeyalli bahu
vrIhi emba samAsa vidhAna baLakeyAgideyendu hELabahudu.

samskxtadalli pItAmbaraH emba jODupada pIta 'haLadi' mattu
ambara 'baTTe' emba eraDu padagaLa jODaNeyinda tayArAgiddu,
adara koneyalli bandiruva visarga as emba pullinga-Ekavacana-
prathamAvibhakti pratyayavannu sUcisuttade. vacana mattu vibhaktigaLannu
sUcisuva pratyayagaLu padarUpa pratyayagaLallade padapratyayagaLalla.
hAgAgi pItAmbaraH emba padadalli pIta mattu ambara emba eraDu
padagaLu mAtra ive. Adare, ivugaLalli ondU I padada kEndra
binduvAgiralu sAdhyavAgadu. yAkendare, I padakke 'haLadi baTTeyannu
uTTiruva vyakti' emba arthavideyallade 'haLadi baTTe' emba arthavilla.
hAgAgi, idara kEndra bindu jODupadada horagiruva vyakti emba
padada mEle bILuttadallade pIta 'haLadi' illavE ambara 'baTTe'
emba jODupadada angavAgiruva padada mEle bILuvudilla. hAgAgi
idu bahuvrIhi emba samAsakke udAharaNeyAgaballudu.

Adare kannaDadalli idakke samAnavAgi tOruva haNegaNNa, calavAdi
modalAda jODupadagaLa koneyalli baruva a illavE i emba
pratyayagaLu padapratyayagaLallade padarUpa pratyayagaLalla. hAgAgi ivu
I jODupadagaLa angagaLAgiruttave. calavAdi emba jODupadadalli
cali mattu vAdi emba eraDu padagaLannu sErisalAgiddu, kEndrabindu
vAdi eraDaneya padada mEle bILuva kAraNa adu tatpuruSakke
udAharaNeyAgaballudallade bahuvrIhige udAharaNeyAgalAradu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


haNegaNNa emba padavU hIgeyE. hosagannaDadalli 'kaNNiruvavanu'
emba arthadalli svatantravAgi kaNNa emba padada prayOgavilladiddarU,
I jODupadadalli antaha padada prayOgavAgideyendU mattu A
padavE adara kEndra binduvAgideyendU illi hELabEkAguttade.

## 5.8.5 avyayIbhAva samAsa
samskxtadalli ondu avyayadondige nAmapadavondannu sErisi racisida
yathASakti, upakxSNam, pratidinam, parOkSam modalAda jODupada
gaLannu avyayibhAvavemba samAsakke udAharaNegaLannAgi koDuvudu
krama. I jODupadagaLu avyayagaLAgi baLakeyAguvuvAda kAraNa,
avugaLa kEndra bindu avugaLa modalaneya angavAgiruva avyayada
mEle bILuttadeyendu hELabahudu. udAharaNegAgi, upakxSNam
emba padakke 'kxSNana hattira' emba arthaviddu, adara kEndra bindu
upa 'hattira' emba padada (avyayada) mEle bILuttade.

kannaDadalli I rIti 'avyaya'gaLAgi baruva hAgU kEndra bindu
modalaneya padada mEle bILuva jODupadagaLilla. Adare, samskxda
avyayIbhAva samAsada innondu vaySiSTyada AdhArada mEle kannaDa
dallU avyayIbhAva samAsavannu kANalu kannaDada kelavaru vayyA
karaNigaLu prayatnisiddAre. yathASakti, upakxSNam modalAda jODu
padagaLa oLanuDiyalli (vigrahavAkyadalli) avyaya nAmapadada balakke
baruttade, Adare jODupadagaLalli ivugaLa sthAnapallaTavAgi, avyaya
nAmapadada eDakke baruttade.

kannaDadalli I rIti jODupadagaLigU mattu avugaLa oLanuDi
gaLigU naDuve angagaLAgi bandiruva padagaLa sthAnadalli badalAvaNe
yannu tOrisuva tudinAlige (nAligeya tudi), hingAlu (kAlina
himbhAga), naDuhagalu (hagalina naDubhAga) modalAdavugaLannu
avyayIbhAva samAsakke udAharaNegaLannAgi hELabahudendu kelavaru
abhiprAyapaTTiddAre.

Adare, I padagaLu samskxtadalli kANisuva hAge avyayagaLalla,
avyayagaLa artha koDuva guNapadagaLU alla. kannaDadalli ivu nAma
padagaLAgi mAtravE baLakeyallive. hAgAgi, ivugaLalli avyayi
bhAvavemba samAsavideyendu vAdisuvudu svalpa kaSTa. I padagaLalli
ondu anga innondu angada 'amSa' (bhAga)vondannu sUcisuvudAda


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


kAraNa ivugaLalliruva samAsavannu 'amSi' embudAgi kareyabahudendu
bEre kelavaru abhiprAyapaTTiddAre.

Adare, idarallU kelavu samasyegaLive. kannaDadalli baruva intaha
ellA jODupadagaLallU I rIti modalaneya anga eraDaneya
angada 'amSa'vondannu gurutisuvudilla. udAharaNegAgi cikkamma
emba pada oLaracaneyalli tudinAlige embudara hAgeyE ide
yAdarU adara modalaneya angavAgi bandiruva cikka emba pada
amma emba eraDaneya pada sUcisuva vyaktiya amSavondannu
sUcisuvudilla (5.6.2(ga) nODi).

eraDaneyadAgi, 'amSi' emba samAsakke kannaDada vayyAkaraNigaLu
udAharaNegaLAgi koDuva jODupadagaLalli kelavannu mAtra (udA:
tudinAlige) 'modalaneya pada pradhAnavAgiruvavugaLu' embudAgi
parigaNisalu sAdhya. uLidavugaLalli pradhAna pada eraDaneyadirabahudu
illavE averaDu padagaLigintalU bhinnavAgiruva horaginadondu pada
virabahudu. hAgAgi, intaha padagaLannu karmadhAraya illavE bahu
vrIhi emba samAsakke mAtravE udAharaNegaLendu hELalu sAdhya.

keLaduTi emba jODupadadalli eraDaneya anga pradhAna pada
vAgide embudannu sAdhisuvudakkAgi kelavaru vayyAkaraNigaLu adakke
tuTiya keLagu embudAgi vigrahavAkyavannu koTTiddAre. Adare nijakkU
kannaDada keLaduTi emba pada bAyiyalliruva eraDu tuTigaLalli
keLaginadannu sUcisuvudallade, tuTiya keLabhAgavannu sUcisuvudilla.
hAgAgi adakke tuTiya keLagu embudakkintalU keLagina tuTi emba
oLanuDiyE sari, mattu I kAraNakkAgi adu karmadhArayakke
udAharaNeyAgaballudallade amSi illavE avyayibhAvakke udA
haraNeyAgalAradu. horabAgilu emba padavU idE rItiyadu.

hingAlu, horamay, naDuhagalu modalAda bEre kelavu
jODupadagaLalli kANisuva angagaLalli yAvudU avugaLa pradhAna
padavAgi illavAda kAraNa, avU kUDa amSi illavE avyayibhAva
samAsakke udAharaNegaLAgalAravu. naDuhagalu emba pada hagalina
naDuviruva ondu bhAgavannu gurutisuvudAda kAraNa, adara anga
gaLAgi bandiruva naDu illavE hagalu emba eraDu padagaLalli
yAvudU adara pradhAna padavenisalAradu. averaDakkintalU bhinnavAda
bhAga emba padada mEle A jODupadada kEndra bindu bILuttade.
hAgAgi adannE A padada pradhAna padavendu parigaNisabEkAguttade,


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


mattu I kAraNakkAgi adannu bahuvrIhi emba samAsakke udAharaNe
yAgi koDabEkAguttade.

## 5.8.6 dvandva samAsa
kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli 'dvandva' emba samAsakke koTTiruva udAharaNe
gaLella padagucchagaLallade jODupadagaLalla. samskxtadalli rAma
lakSmaNa, mAtApitara modalAdavugaLannu jODupadagaLendu
kareyalu avugaLa angagaLAgiruva padagaLalli koneyadarondige mAtra
vibhakti pratyayagaLu baruvuvembudE kAraNa. kannaDada rAmalakSmaNaru,
aNNatammandiru embantahavugaLalli idE rItiyalli vibhaktipratyaya
koneya padadondige mAtra baruvudAda kAraNa (udA: rAmalakSmaNa
rannu) avannu dvandvasamAsakke udAharaNegaLannAgi koDalAgide.

Adare kannaDadalli samskxtada hAge vibhakti pratyayada baLakeya
AdhArada mEle jODupadagaLannu padagucchagaLinda bErpaDisalu sAdhya
vAgadembudannu nAvu mEleyE (5.8.2ralli) nODiruvevu. kannaDada
rAmalakSmaNaru embantaha baLakegaLalli eraDu nAmapadagaLannu oTTu
sErisi bahuvacana pratyayadondige hELalAgideyallade avannu ondE
padavAgi parivartisilla. avugaLa arthavannU nEravAgi avugaLa oLa
racaneyindalEnE paDeyalu sAdhyavide. hAgAgi ivu jODupadagaLalla.

## 5.8.7 gamaka samAsa
kannaDakkEnE viSiSTavAduvendu hELuva gamaka mattu kriyAsamAsagaLa
avastheyU idE rItiyadu. avugaLige vayyAkaraNigaLu koDuva
ippattaydu, kiriya maga, tUguva toTTilu, kanDa vicAra moda
lAda udAharaNegaLella bariya padagucchagaLallade jODupadagaLalla.
avugaLalli eraDu padagaLu oTTige bandiveyEnO nija; Adare avu
oTTu sEri ondE padavAgilla. endare, avu kannaDada vAkyaracaneya
niyamagaLige anusAravAgi oTTu sEriveyallade, padaracaneya niyama
gaLige anusAravAgi oTTu sErilla.

kannaDada vayyAkaraNigaLu illiyU mEle karmadhAraya samAsada
viSayadalli mADiruvantaha tappannE mADiddAre (5.8.2 nODi).
kannaDa mattu samskxta bhASegaLa naDuve vAkyaracaneyalli kANisuva
atyanta prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsavondannu avaru sariyAgi artha
mADikonDilla embudE idakke kAraNa. kriyApadagaLa sambandhaka rUpa


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


vannu (mADuva, mADida, mADada embantaha kriyArUpagaLannu)
baLasuvalli I eraDu bhASegaLu hEge bhinnavAgive embudannu keLagina
vAkyagaLinda tiLiyabahudu.

1. (12ka) tatra EkaH mxtaH sarpaH asti.
2. alli ondu satta hAvu ide.
4. (13ka) rAmaH Ekam mxtam sarpa0 apaSyat.
5. rAma ondu satta hAvannu nODida.
7. (14ka) rAmaH EkEna mxtEna sarpENa bhItaH.
8. rAma ondu satta hAvige hedarida.
10. (15ka) rAmaH Ekasya mxtasya sarpasya upari pAdam nikSipat.
11. rAma ondu satta hAvina mEle kAlirisida.

mElina vAkyagaLalli mxtaH embudu samskxtada 'kxdanta' emba
hesarina sambandhaka kriyArUpa (adu sAyuva ghaTaneyannu sarpaH
'hAvu' embudarondige sambandhisuttade); idE kelasavannu mADuvuda
kkAgi kannaDadalli satta emba rUpa baLakeyallide. ivugaLalli samskxtada
mxtaH embudu bEre bEre vAkyagaLalli bEre bEre linga-vacana-
vibhaktigaLondige bandideyAdare, kannaDada satta embudu ellA vAkya
gaLallU ondE rUpadalli bandide.

kannaDadalli samskxtada hAge sambandhakagaLige linga-vacana-vibhakti
pratyayagaLannu sErisuva avaSyakateyilla mAtravalla, hAge sErisalu
sAdhyavU illa. idakke kAraNavEnendare, kannaDadalli sambandhakagaLu
guNapadagaLa hAge baLakeyAguttavallade samskxtadalliruvante nAma
padagaLa hAge baLakeyAguvudilla. nAmapadagaLa hAge baLakeyAgalu
avakke avanu, adu modalAda sarvanAmagaLannu sErisikoLLabEkAgu
ide (udA: sattudannu, sattudakke, sattudarinda, sattudaralli,
ityAdi).

samskxtada sambandhaka kriyArUpagaLannu avakke linga-vacana-vibhakti
pratyayagaLannu sErisadeyU baLasalu sAdhyavide. Adare antaha baLake
gaLannu mEle koTTiruva baLakegaLinda bhinnavAdavugaLendu tOrisuvu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


dakkAgi jODupadagaLendu parigaNisuva avaSyakateyide. intaha baLake
gaLannu keLagina (kha) vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.

1. (12kha) tatra EkaH mxtasarpaH asti.
2. alli ondu satta hAvu ide.
4. (13kha) rAmaH Ekam mxtasarpa0 apaSyat.
5. rAma ondu satta hAvannu nODida.
7. (14kha) rAmaH EkEn mxtasarpENa bhItaH.
8. rAma ondu satta hAvige hedarida.
10. (15kha) rAmaH Ekasya mxtasarpasya upari pAdam nikSipat.
11. rAma ondu satta hAvina mEle kAlirisida.

mEle (12kha-15kha)gaLalli koTTiruva ellA samskxta vAkya
gaLallU mxta emba sambandhaka (kxdanta) rUpa linga-vacana-vibhakti
pratyayavillade nEravAgi sarpa emba nAmapadadondige
bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. idakke modalE koTTiruva (12ka-15ka)
vAkyagaLalli I padadondige bEre bEre vibhaktipratyayagaLu bandiddu,
avu illi biddu hOgiruvudu samskxtada maTTige ondu padaracaneya
niyamavendu vayyAkaraNigaLa abhiprAyapaTTiddAre, mattu I
kAraNakkAgi mxtasarpa emba padadalli mxta mattu sarpa emba
eraDu padagaLu samAsavemba padaracaneya vidhAnada mUlaka
oTTusEriveyendu avaru vAdisu ttAre.

kannaDada satta hAvu embudu (12kha-15kha)gaLalli idara
hAgeyE kANisuvudAdarU adu ondu padagucchavallade jODupada
valla. yAkendare, illi satta emba pada linga-vacana-vibhakti pratyaya
gaLondige bAradiruvudakke mEle sUcisiruvante kAraNa bEreyE ide.
kannaDakkU samskxtakkU naDuviruva I prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsavannu
sariyAgi arthamADikoLLadiruvudE I rIti kriyApadagaLa sambandhaka
rUpagaLannoLagonDiruva padagucchagaLannu gamaka samAsadalli bandiruva
jODupadagaLendu bhAvisalu kAraNavirabEku.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


## 5.8.8 kriyAsamAsa
samskxtadallillada kriyAsamAsavemba innondu rItiya padaracaneya
vidhAnavU kannaDadallideyendu adare vayyAkaraNigaLu hELiruvudu
intahadE kAraNadinda endu hELabahudu. maravEru, kaymugi, nidde
mADu modalAdavugaLannu I samAsakke udAharaNegaLannAgi koDa
lAgide. Adare illi modalaneya padadondige bandidda annu emba
vibhakti pratyaya bidduhOgiruvudu kannaDada ondu vAkyaracaneya
niyamada AdhArada mElallade, padaracaneya niyamada AdhArada
mElalla.

idallade, kriyApadadondige baruva I nAmapadagaLannu vAkyada
itara sthAnagaLige vargAyisidAga, illavE avugaLondige ottihELuva
arthaviruva U emba pratyayavannu baLasidAga, hIge biddu hOda
annu emba pratyaya punaH kANisikoLLuttade. udA:

1. (16ka) rAju ninne sariyAgi nidde mADiralilla.
2. (16kha) rAju ninne niddeyannu sariyAgi mADiralilla.
4. (17ka) rAju dEvarige hUhAki kaymugida.
5. (17kha) rAju dEvarige hUvannU hAkida, kayyannU mugida.

jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi baruva padagaLannu I rIti vAkyadalli bEre
sthAnagaLige vargAyisalu illavE avugaLalli modalinadarondige U
emba ottihELuva pratyayavannu sErisi baLasalu sAdhyavAgadembudannu
illi gamanisabahudu.

kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva bEre kelavu kriyApadagaLalli (udA:
marehogu) I rIti modalaneya angadondige annu emba pratyaya
vannu baLasalu sAdhyavAgadirabahudu. Adare ivannu jODupadagaLendu
parigaNisade nuDigaTTugaLendu parigaNisuvudE uttama. samAsavemba
padaracaneya vidhAnada mUlaka 'jODu'kriyApadagaLannu tayArisa
diralu kAraNavEnembudannu Araneya adhyAyadalli vivarisalAgide.

## 5.9 sArAmSa
eraDu padagaLannu oTTige sErisi ondE padavAgi mADiruva nAmapada
gaLannu jODupadagaLendu kareyabahudu. kannaDadalli intaha padagaLu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


halaviddu, avugaLalli eraDaneya anga heccina kaDegaLallU nAmapada
vAgiruttade. modalaneya anga mAtra nAmapadavirabahudu, kriyApada
virabahudu illavE guNapadavirabahudu. I viSayavannu baLasi kannaDada
jODupadagaLannu mUru mukhya gumpugaLAgi vingaDisalu sAdhyavide.

ivattina kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva jODupadagaLa varNane
gaLu (mattu avugaLa tayArikeyalli baLasiruva samAsa emba pada
racaneya vidhAnada varNanegaLu) I viSayakke jAsti gamana koTTilla.
idakke badalu, samskxta vyAkaraNagaLannanusarisi, jODupadada anga
gaLAgi bandiruva padagaLalli yAvudu 'pradhAna pada' emba viSayakke
avu heccina gamana koTTive. idarindAgi avugaLalli baruva jODupada
gaLa varNane kannaDada maTTige aSTondu txptikaravAgilla.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


<a id="adhyAya-6"></a><a id="kriyA-padagaLa-oLaracane"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-6) | [English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-6--internal-structure-of-verbs)

## adhyAya ArukriyApadagaLa oLaracane

## O.1 pIThike
kannaDada kriyApadagaLannU nAmapadagaLa hAge oLaracaneyiruvavugaLu
mattu illadavugaLu embudAgi eraDu vargagaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhya
vide. udAharaNegAgi, mundAgu emba kriyApadadalli munde emba
guNapadavU mattu Agu emba kriyApadavU sErikonDive; hambalisu
emba kriyApadadalli hambala emba nAmapadavU mattu isu emba
pratyayavU sErikonDive.

nAmapadagaLigU mattu kriyApadagaLigU naDuviruva ondu mukhya
vyatyAsavEnendare, oLaracaneyiruva kriyApadagaLa arthavannu heccina
sandarbhagaLallU nEravAgi avugaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva padagaLa
illavE pratyayagaLa sahAyadinda paDeyalu sAdhyavide. idakke kelavE
kelavu apavAdagaLiddu, avannu 'nuDigaTTu'gaLendu parigaNisalu sAdhya
vide. oLaracaneyiruva nAmapadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisuvantaha jODu
pada mattu padaguccha emba bhEda (5.2 nODi) oLaracaneyiruva I
kriyApadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisuvudilla.

## 6.1.1 kriyApadagaLa kelasa
nAmapadagaLigU mattu kriyApadagaLigU naDuve avugaLa oLaracane
yalli kANisuva I prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsakke avu vAkyadalli naDesa
bEkAgiruva kelasagaLu bEre bErAgiruvudE mukhya kAraNa. nAmapada
gaLu vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisabEkAgideyAda kAraNa,
avugaLannu hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu embudAgi eraDu bEre

© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


bEre vidhAnagaLalli baLasalu sAdhyavAguttade. sAmAnyavAgi, avannu
nEravAgi baLasidAgalella avu hesarisuva kelasavannU mattu padaguccha
gaLa rUpadalli baLasidAga varNisuva kelasavannU naDesuttaveyembudannu
nAvu mUraneya adhyAyadalli nODiruvevu.

vAkyagaLalli kriyApadagaLu naDesabEkAgiruva kelasa idakkinta tIra
bhinnavAdudu. avu vAkyada pradhAna padavAgi bEre bEre rItiya ghaTane
gaLannu varadi mADabEkAguttade, illavE kELuvudu, bEDuvudu,
bayasuvudu, allagaLeyuvudu modalAda bEre bEre rItiya
'mAtina kelasa'gaLalli avannu toDagisabEkAguttade. kriyApadagaLu
naDesa balla intaha bEre bEre rItiya kelavu mAtina kelasagaLannu
keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.

1. (1ka) rAju pETege hOgiddAne.
2. (1kha) rAju pETege hOgiddAnO?
3. (1ga) rAju pETege hOgali.
4. (1gha) rAju pETege hOgalilla.
5. (1ja) rAju pETege hOgabAradu.

intaha bEre bEre rItiya mAtina kelasagaLalli baruva ghaTanegaLu vyakti,
vastu modalAdavugaLa hAge sthAyi (endare badalAgada) rUpada
lliruva badalu asthAyi rUpadalliruttave. hAgAgi, vyakti, vastu
modalAdavugaLige nAmapadagaLa mUlaka hesarugaLannu koDuva hAge,
ghaTanegaLige kriyApadagaLa mUlaka hesarugaLannu koDalu sAdhya
vAguvudilla. varNaneyembudondE avugaLa baLakeyalli kANisi
koLLuva vidhAna. I kAraNakkAgi oLaracaneyiruva kriyApadagaLa artha
vannu heccina sandarbhagaLallU nEravAgi avugaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva
pada mattu pratyayagaLa arthadindalEnE paDeyalu sAdhyavAguttade.

nAmapadagaLannu prAmukhyavAgi ankitanAma mattu rUDhanAma
embudAgi eraDu vargagaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhya embudannu nAvu
(3.5)ralli nODiruvevu. avu hesarisuva pratiyondu vyakti, vastu
modalAduvakkU bEre bEre sandarbhagaLalli sambandhitavAgiveyAdare
ankitanAmagaLu mattu oTTige ondE bAri sambandhitavAgiveyAdare
rUDhanAmagaLu embudAgi I eraDu rItiya nAmapadagaLa naDuviruva
mukhya vyatyAsavannu vivarisi hELabahudu.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


Adare kriyApadagaLannu I rIti ankitakriye mattu rUDhakriye
embudAgi vingaDisalu sAdhyavAgadu. avu kriyegaLannu hesarisuvudakkAgi
baLakeyAguva badalu nirdESisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttiruvudE I
rIti eraDu rItiya kriyApadagaLilladiruvudakke mukhya kAraNa.

## 6.1.2 kriyAsamAsa
kannaDadalli kriyAsamAsa embudAgi ondu viSiSTavAda samAsavide
yendu kannaDada vayyAkaraNigaLu abhiprAyapaTTiddAre. Adare I abhi
prAyakke AdhAravAgi avaru koDuva kaymugi, maravEru modalAda
udAharaNegaLella nijakkU jODupadagaLalla, bariya padagucchagaLu
mAtra embudannu hindina adhyAyadalli (5.8.8ralli) nODiruvevu.
samAsavemba vyAkaraNa vidhAnavannu nAvu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisuvudakkAgi mAtra baLasuttEve. kriyApadagaLa mUlaka ghaTane
gaLannu hesarisabEkAguvudillavAda kAraNa avugaLa tayArikeyalli
samAsavemba vidhAnakke yAva sthAnavU illa.

kriyApadagaLu tiLisuva ghaTaneyinda bAdhitavAguva vyakti, vastu
modalAduvannu sUcisuvudakkAgi kannaDadalli nAmapadadondige annu
emba vibhakti pratyayavannu baLasuva kramavide. Adare, I pratyaya
vannoLagonDiruva nAmapada kriyApadada hattira bandAgalella kriyA
padakkU nAmapadakkU naDuve hattirada sambandhaviruvudannu sUcisalu
A pratyaya biddu hOguvudE jAsti. vyaktigaLannu gurutisuva nAmapada
gaLalli mAtra I rIti annu emba pratyaya biddu hOguvudilla.

1. (2ka) sarale maguvannu tUguttiddALe.
2. (2kha) Ake akkiyinda kallu hekkuttiddALe.
3. (2ga) avanu maysUrininda ondu Ane tandiddAne.

(2ka)dalli annu emba pratyaya vyaktiyondannu sUcisuva magu emba
padadondige bandideyAda kAraNa kriyApadada hattiravE iddarU
biddu hOgilla. Adare (2kha-ga)gaLalli kallu mattu Ane emba
padagaLinda idu biddu hOgide.

I nAmapadagaLannu vAkyadallEnE bEre kaDegaLige vargAyisidAga
(keLage koTTiruva (3ka-kha) vAkyagaLannu nODi), illavE avu
gaLondige ottukoDuva E emba pratyaya athavA 'mattu' emba


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


arthada U emba pratyayavannu sErisi hELidAga (4ka-ga nODi),
biddu hOgiruva I vibhakti pratyaya punaH kANisikoLLuttade.

1. (3ka) rAju ondu lOTa nIru kuDida.
2. (3kha) ondu lOTa nIrannu rAju kuDida.
4. (4ka) rAju svalpa hottu pATha Odali.
5. (4kha) rAju svalpa hottu pAThavannE Odali.
6. (4ga) rAju svalpa hottu pAThavannU Odali.

I kAraNakkAgi, kannaDadalli kaymugi (kayyannu mugi), maravEru
(maravannu Eru), karenIDu (kareyannu nIDu) embantaha kriyApada
gaLalli annu emba vibhakti pratyaya biddu hOgiruvudu samAsavemba
padaracaneya niyamadindalla, mEle sUcisiruva vAkyaracaneya niyama
dinda endu hELalu sAdhyavide.

nAmapada illavE guNapadadondige kriyApada sEri jODupada
vAgiruvante kANisuva bEreyU kelavu padagaLu kannaDadallive. ivannu
jODupadagaLendu kareyuvudakkintalU 'kUDupada'vemba bErondu
hesarininda kareyuvudE oLLeyadembudannu munde 6.4ralli nODaliru
vevu. jODupadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisuva atyanta prAmukhyavAda
guNadharmagaLAvuvU I kUDupadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisadiruvudE
avannu I rIti jODupadagaLinda bhinnavAdavugaLendu parigaNisalu
kAraNa.

## 6.2 oLaracaneyillada kriyApadagaLu
mEle sUcisiruvante, kannaDadalli baLakeyAguva kriyApadagaLige oLa
racaneyirabahudu athavA illadirabahudu. ivugaLalli oLaracaneyilla
diruva aLu, koDu, kali, mare modalAda kriyApadagaLannu
'kriyAdhAtu'gaLendu kareyabahudu. intaha padagaLannu avugaLalli
baruva akSaragaLa sankhye mattu svarUpagaLa AdhArada mEle mattu
avugaLa koneya svarada AdhArada mEle bEre bEre vibhAgagaLAgi
vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. intaha vingaDaNe avugaLondige barabahudAda
pratyayagaLa svarUpavannu mattu I rIti pratyayagaLu sEridAga avu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


gaLalli illavE pratyayagaLalli kANisikoLLuva badalAvaNegaLannu varNisu
valli sahAyakavAguttade.

kriyAdhAtugaLannu ekAradalli konegoLLuvavu, ikAradalli kone
goLLuvavu mattu ukAradalli konegoLLuvavu embudAgi mUru
vargagaLalli vingaDisuvudu kannaDada maTTige ondu prAmukhyavAda
vingaDaNe. ekAra mattu ikAradalli konegoLLuva kriyAdhAtugaLella
eraDakSaradavugaLAgiddu avugaLalli baruva akSaragaLeraDU laghuvAgiru
ttave (endare, avugaLalli uddasvara, ottakSara illavE sonne kANisuvu
dilla). udA:

baraballa kriyAdhAtugaLigU illi udAharaNegaLannAgi koDalAgide.

## 6.3 kelavu paLeyuLikegaLu
hosagannaDa kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyalli isu emba ondu pratyaya
vannu biTTare (idU kUDa haLegannaDada kAladalli ondu kriyApada
vAgittu), bEre pratyayagaLa baLakeyE illavendU hELalu sAdhyavide.

I mAtige apavAdavAgi kelavu paLeyaLikegaLannu mEle koTTiruva
'kriyAdhAtu'gaLalli kANabahudu. ivella kannaDa, tamiLu, telugu,
gOnDi, kuyi, kuDukh modalAda bhASegaLige mUlavAgidda


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


'drAviDa'bhASeya kriyApadagaLalli iddirabahudAda oLaracaneya paLe
yaLikegaLu. ivugaLalli kelavannu pratyayagaLendu hELalu kannaDadallEnE
adhAra siguvudAdarU kannaDada vyAkaraNadalli ivakke heccina prAdhAnya
villa.

I mUla bhASeyalli kriyAdhAtugaLella ondE akSaradavugaLAgi
iddirabEkendu bEre bEre drAviDa bhASegaLannu hOlisi naDesida
cAritrika abhyAsada AdhArada mEle hELalu sAdhyavide. I ondakSarada
dhAtugaLalli heccinavU bEre bEre pratyayagaLondige sErikonDu
eraDu mattu mUru akSaradavugaLAgive. haLegannaDadalli intaha kelavu
ondakSarada dhAtugaLu kANisuttaveyAdarU hosagannaDadalli avellavU
eraDakSaradavugaLAgive (udA: ir-iru, sOl-sOlu, kAy-
kAyu, ityAdi).

hosagannaDadalli baruva kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embu
dannu vivarisuvAga, avu I rIti ondakSarada dhAtugaLige pratyayagaLu
sEruvudara mUlaka beLedu bandavugaLemba cAritrika viSayavannu
pariSIlisuva avaSyakateyillavAdarU, adannu pratibimbisuvantaha kelavu
amSagaLannu gamanisadiralu sAdhyavAgadu. udAharaNegAgi, mUru
akSaragaLiruva kriyAdhAtugaLalli kelavu eraDu akSaraviruva kriyAdhAtu
gaLige illavE bEre mUru akSaragaLiruva kriyAdhAtugaLige sambandhisi
dantiddu, avugaLalli baruva mUraneya akSara ondu pratyayavAgiru
vante tOruttade. intaha kelavu pratyayagaLannu keLagina vibhAgagaLalli
koDalAgide.

## Ta.kha.ga cu emba pratyaya
cu emba akSaradalli konegoLLuva tirucu, nuNucu, eracu, kaLacu
modalAda kelavu kriyApadagaLa koneyalli kANisuva cu embudu
ondu pratyayavirabahudu endu vAdisalu I keLagina hOlikegaLu
AdhAravAgaballuvu. illi hOlikegAgi kriyApadagaLannu mAtravallade
nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLannU koDalAgide.

## 6.4 isu emba pratyayada baLake
mEle koTTiruvantaha paLeyaLikegaLAgi uLidiruva pratyayagaLannu
biTTare, kannaDa kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyalli pratyayagaLa baLakeyE
illavendU hELalu sAdhyavide. Adare idakke apavAdavAgi, kannaDada
kelavu kriyApadagaLalli isu emba ondu pratyaya kANisikoLLuttade.

vondu sandarbhagaLalli ivugaLa baLakeyannu kANabahudu. udA:

guNapadagaLannU tayArisalu sAdhyavide.

innu kelavu isu embudaralli konegoLLuva padagaLu kriyApada

uLidilla. udA:

kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyalli baruva I isu emba padapratyaya
vannE hOluva padarUpa pratyayavondu kannaDadalli baLakeyallide.
idannu kriyApadavondakke sErisi, 'adu sUcisuva kelasavannu bEre
yavara mUlaka naDesalAgide' emba 'prEraNArtha'vannu paDeyalu sAdhya
vAguttade (udA: mADu-mADisu, tinnu-tinnisu, bILu-bILisu,
ityAdi). I eraDu pratyayagaLa rUpa ondE AdarU avugaLalli
modalaneyadu mAtra padaracanege sambandhisidudu embudannu illi
gamanisuvudu avaSya.

## 6.5 kUDupadagaLu
Agu, ADu, koDu, biDu, kaccu, bILu, mADu, hAku modalAda
kelavu viSiSTavAda kriyApadagaLondige itara kriyApadagaLannu sErisi
'kUDupada'gaLannu tayArisuva vidhAnavondu kannaDadalli baLakeyallide.
I kriyApadagaLondige bEre kriyApadagaLannu mAtravallade, nAmapada


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


illavE guNapadagaLannu sErisiyU intaha kUDupadagaLannu tayAri
salu sAdhyavide. I keLagina kelavu oLaracaneyiruva kriyApadagaLannu I
vidhAnakke udAharaNegaLannAgi koDabahudu.

hoDedADu bobbehAku aDDabILu
kanDubaru mAtukoDu mundUDu
ODADu bErubiDu hALAgu

## 6.5.1 koDupadagaLu mattu jODupadagaLu
intaha oLaracaneyiruva kriyApadagaLannu jODupadagaLendu kareyade
'kUDupada'gaLemba bEreyE ondu hesarininda kareyalu jODupada
gaLigU mattu nAmapadagucchagaLigU naDuve arthadalli illavE baLake
yalli kANisuvantaha vyatyAsagaLu (3.2 nODi) I kriyApadagaLigU
mattu kriyApadagucchagaLigU naDuve kANisadiruvudE mukhya kAraNa.
nijakkU ivannu kriyApadagaLendu kareyade kriyApadagucchagaLendu kare
yalU sAdhyavide.

mEle mUraneya adhyAyadalli vivarisiruvante, jODupadagaLa
arthavannu nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle nirdharisi
hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. avu gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa
guNadharmada AdhArada mEle mAtravE avugaLa arthavannu nirdharisalu
sAdhya. Adare kUDupadagaLAgi baruva kriyApadagaLa arthavannu
nirdharisuvalli intaha samasyeyilla. heccinaDegaLalliyU avugaLa artha
vannu nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mElEnE nirdharisi
hELalu sAdhyavide. idakke kelavu apavAdagaLiveyEnO nija; Adare
illU jODupada mattu padagucchagaLa naDuve avugaLa baLakeyalli
kANisuvantaha vyatyAsavilla.

kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyalli I rIti jODupadagaLiginta bhinna
vAda 'kUDupada' embudara baLake kANisuvudakke nAmapadagaLa hAge
avannu hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu emba eraDu vidhAnagaLalli
baLasalu sAdhyavAgadiruvudE mukhya kAraNa. kriyApadagaLu ghaTanegaLannu
nirdESisuttavallade gurutisuvudilla. avu EnAyitu (yAva ghaTane
jaragitu) embudannu nEravAgi tiLisuttavallade, ghaTaneyondannu
gurutisi (hesarisi illavE varNisi), anantara A ghaTaneya kuritAgi
EnAyitu (adu naDeyitE, naDeyalillavE, naDeyabahudE, ityAdi


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


yAgi) embudannu tiLisalu prayatnisuvudilla. hAgAgi, avugaLa baLake
yalli hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu emba vyatyAsa kANisalu sAdhya
villa.

## Ta.ji.2 koDupadagaLa racane
kUDupadagaLalli eraDu (athavA jAsti) padagaLu oTTu sEriruttave.
ivugaLalli yAvAgalU koneya pada kriyApadavAgiruvudu avaSya.
mEleyE sUcisiruvante, ivugaLa modalaneya pada kriyApadavira
bahudu, nAmapadavirabahudu, illavE guNapadavirabahudu.

idallade, ivugaLa modalaneya angavAgi bandiruva kriyApadavu
dhAtu rUpadallirabahudu, illavE adara yAvudAdarondu kriyA
padarUpadallirabahudu. udAharaNegAgi, kuNidADu, kanDubaru,
tEli biDu, hOgalADisu modalAda kUDupadagaLalli kuNidu,
kanDu, tEli, hOgalu modalAda kriyApadarUpagaLu modalaneya
angavAgi bandive. aparUpavAgi nAmapadagaLU avugaLa vibhakti
rUpadalli intaha kUDupadagaLa modalaneya angavAgi baraballu
vembudakke mAtanADu (mAtannu ADu) emba udAharaNeyannu
koDabahudu.

kUDupadagaLa modalaneya angavAgi baruva nAmapada kannaDaddE
irabahudu, athavA ingliS modalAda bEre bhASegaLinda eravalAgi
bandudirabahudu. bandAgu, sTArT‌mADu, duHkhavAgu modalA
duvannu idakke udAharaNegaLannAgi koDabahudu. I rIti eravalAgi
banda padagaLu bahaLa sulabhavAgi intaha kUDupadagaLalli sErikoLLu
ttaveyembudu avakkU mattu jODupadagaLigU naDuviruva innondu
prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsa.

kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva kUDupadagaLannu I keLage avugaLa
koneyalli baruva kriyApadagaLa pariSIlaneya mUlaka vivarisalu
yatnisalAgide.

## (ka) Agu
I kriyApadavannu mukhyavAgi nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLondige
baLasi kUDupadagaLannu racisalu sAdhyavide. intaha kUDupadagaLallella
Agu emba kriyApadakke adaradE arthaviddu, kUDupadagaLa arthavannu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneya sahAyadindalE paDeyalu sAdhya
embudannu gamanisabahudu.

ukAradalli konegoLLuva padagaLondige I kriyApada bandAga
avugaLa koneyalliruva ukAra biddu hOguttade. Adare itara pada
gaLondige bandAga I rIti koneya svara biddu hOguvudilla. idakke
badalu, avugaLa koneyalli ikAra illavE ekAravideyAdalli A
eraDu padagaLa naDuve yakAra bandu sErikoLLuttade, mattu avugaLa
koneyalli akAravideyAdalli vakAra sErikoLLuttade. guNapada
gaLondige I kriyApada bandiruvAga mAtra kelavomme I niyamakke
apavAdavAgi guNapadagaLa koneya akAra illavE ekAra bidduhOgu
vudannu kANabahudu.

1. (1) nAmapadagaLondige baLake
2. peTTAgu baliyAgu guNavAgu
3. siTTAgu guriyAgu taDavAgu
4. nIrAgu eDeyAgu mAyavAgu
5. ondAgu
7. (2) guNapadagaLondige baLake
8. hALAgu baDavAgu mundAgu
9. kappAgu kappagAgu mElAgu
10. idirAgu aDDAgu
12. (3) itara padagaLondige baLake
13. Agu emba I kriyApada sAmAnyavAgi bEre kriyApadagaLondige
14. kUDupadagaLalli baLakeyAguvudilla. Adare, aniyamita rUpagaLiruva
15. bEku, bEDu, sAku, illi embantahavugaLondige, mattu kriyApada
16. gaLa sthAnadalli baruva sari, tappu, suLLu embantahavugaLondige sEri
17. idu kUDupadagaLalli baraballudu. udA:
19. bEkAgu tappAgu
20. sAkAgu sariyAgu
21. bEDavAgu suLLAgu
22. illavAgu unTAgu

ingliS‌nantaha bEre bhASegaLinda eravalAgi banda kriyApada
gaLannu kriyApadada sthAnadalli baLasuvudakkAgi kannaDadalli avugaLondige
Agu mattu mADu emba eraDu kriyApadagaLannu sErisi kUDupada
gaLAgi mADi baLasuva vidhAna baLakeyallide. ivugaLalli Agu embudu
ondu ghaTaneyannU mattu mADu embudu ondu kelasavannU tiLisu
ttave. (udA: sTArTAgu, sTArT‌mADu, dipressAgu, kavnT
mADu, ityAdi).

## (kha) ADu
I kriyApadavannu baLasi racisuva kUDupadagaLannu kriyApada, nAma
pada illavE guNapadagaLinda tayArisalu sAdhyavide. kriyApadagaLannu
sAmAnyavAgi avugaLa 'bhUtanyUna' rUpadalli baLasuvudu rUDhi.
intaha kUDupadagaLalli ADu emba kriyApadakke ondu ghaTane halavu
bAri athavA bahaLa hottu naDeyuvudemba artha baruttade.
sAmAnyavAgi idu calaneyannu sUcisuvantaha nali, kuNi, tirugu,
hAru, ODu, tElu, tUgu, horaLu modalAda
kriyApadagaLondige baruttade. udA:

yAdarU adara kUDupadavAda nagADu embudaralli adu dhAtu
rUpadallE bandiruvudannu gamanisabahudu.

spaSTapaDisuttave. Adare kriyApadagaLa bhUtanyUnarUpadondige baLasi

embudu) adakke I baLakeyalli baruvudilla. udA:

(an) emba vibhakti pratyayadondige bandiruvudannu kANabahudu.
idondu aniyamitavAda baLake.

ADu emba kriyApada guNapadagaLondigU kUDupadagaLalli bara
balludu embudakke keLagina udAharaNegaLannu koDabahudu.

hitakkAgi mADuvudemba artha idakkideyAda kAraNa, antaha
arthavannu koDaballa kriyApadagaLondige mAtra idu baraballudu.
idarondige kriyApadagaLu avugaLa bhUtanyUnarUpadalli baruttave.

## 6.5.3 bEre kelavu kriyApadagaLa baLake
intaha kUDupadagaLalli eraDaneya kriyApadavAgi kANisuva itara
kriyApadagaLalli prAmukhyavAdavugaLu I keLaginavu. ivugaLalli kelavu
(udA: mADu, keDu, ettu) nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLondige

I kriyApadagaLalli keDu embudara modalaneya akSaradalliruva
kakAra gakAravAgiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. intaha sErikeya badalA
vaNegaLu bEre kelavu kUDupadagaLallU kANisuttave. kelavu kriyApada
gaLalli ivu niyamitavAgi ellA kUDupadagaLallU kANisuvuvAdare
(udA: kANu-gANu, kuTTu-guTTu, kedaru-gedaru), bEre kelavu
kriyApadagaLalli aniyamitavAgi kANisikoLLuttave (udA: kaTTu-gaTTu,
kaLe-gaLe, tirugu-dirugu). udA:

kiruguTTu konegANu kaLegundu
busuguTTu managANu edegundu

baDambaDu taDegaTTi hindirugu
baLapaDu aDDakaTTu taletirugu

mEle koTTiruva kriyApadagaLu mAtravallade bEreyU halavAru
kriyApadagaLu intaha kUDupadagaLa eraDaneya padavAgi baraballu
vembudannu I keLagina udAharaNegaLinda tiLiyabahudu.

## O.O sArAmSa
kannaDada kriyApadagaLa oLaracaneyalli isu embudannu biTTare bEre
pratyayagaLa baLake bahaLa aparUpa. paLeyaLikegaLAgiruva kelavu pratyaya
gaLannu mAtra avugaLalli kANalu sAdhyavide. idallade nAmapadagaLa
oLaracaneyalli kANisuvantaha jODupadagaLa baLakeyU kriyApadagaLa
llilla. kannaDa vayyAkaraNigaLu varNisuva kriyAsamAsavembavugaLu
nijakkU padagucchagaLallade jODupada(samastapada)gaLalla.

kriyApadagaLa bhUtanyUna rUpadondige mattu kelavu nAmapada
mattu guNapadagaLondige kelavu viSiSTavAda kriyApadagaLannu baLasi
'kUDupada'gaLemba aDakavAda padagucchagaLannu tayArisi baLasuvudu
kannaDada kriyApadagaLa innondu vaySiSTya.

<a id="adhyAya-7"></a><a id="guNa-padagaLa-oLaracane"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-7) | [English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-7--internal-structure-of-qualifiers)

adhyAya ELu
guNapadagaLa oLaracane

## 7.1 pIThike
nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLiginta bhinnavAgiruva 'guNapada'gaLemba
bEreyE ondu padavargakke sEruva padagaLu kannaDadalliveyembudannu
nAvu eraDaneya adhyAyadalli nODiruvevu. I padagaLu vAkyadalli
baruva vidhAna, tegedukoLLuva pratyayagaLu mattu sUcisuva artha
emba I mUru viSayagaLallU nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLiginta
bhinnavAgiveyembudannU nODiruvevu. oLaracaneyallU I padagaLu
nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLiginta bhinnavAgiveyembudannu I adhyAya
dalli nODaliruvevu.

kannaDa vAkyagaLalli mukhyavAgi eraDu rItiya guNapadagaLu baLake
yAguttave. avugaLalli kelavu nAmapadagaLondige baraballuvu mattu
innu kelavu kriyApadagaLondige baraballuvu. nAmapadagaLondige
baraballa udda, biLi, doDDa, modalAda guNapadagaLu nAmapadagaLu
gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa guNadharmagaLannu sUcisu
vuvAdare, kriyApadagaLondige baraballa mEle, hinde, mellage,
modalAda guNapadagaLu kriyApadagaLu nirdESisuva ghaTanegaLa guNa
dharmagaLannu sUcisuttave.

(1) doDDa peTTigeyannu keLage irisiddEne.

(2) hosa baTTeyannu haLE baTTeya hAge jAsti
nenasabEDa.

mEle koTTiruva (1-2) vAkyagaLalli doDDa, hosa mattu haLE
emba guNapadagaLu avugaLa anantara bandiruva nAmapadagaLa guNa

© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


dharmagaLannU mattu keLage mattu jAsti emba guNapadagaLu avugaLa
anantara bandiruva kriyApadagaLa guNadharmagaLannU sUcisuttave.

I eraDu rItiya guNapadagaLa naDuve avugaLa arthadalli mAtra
vallade, oLaracaneyalli mattu vAkyadalli avakkiruva svAtantryadalli
vyatyAsagaLiveyembudannu munde nODaliruvevu.

idallade, guNapadagaLondige baraballa bahaLa, barI, balu,
modalAda bEre kelavu guNapadagaLU kannaDadalli baLakeyallive. ivu
guNapadagaLu sUcisuva guNadharmagaLa pramANavannu tiLisuttave. udA:

(3) I baTTe bahaLa teLLagide.

(4) avanu bhArI doDDa mane kaTTisuttiddAne.

Adare intaha guNapadagaLa sankhye jAstiyilla. idallade, ivugaLa
oLaracaneyalli hELuvantaha viSiSTavAda sangatiyEnU illavAda
kAraNa, nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLondige baraballa eraDu rItiya
guNapadagaLa oLaracaneyannu mAtravE I adhyAyadalli svalpa
vivaravAgi pariSIlisalAgide.

## 7.2 kelavu vyatyAsagaLu
nAmapadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLu sAmAnyavAgi bEgane
badalAgadiruva 'sthAyI' guNadharmagaLannU mattu kriyApadagaLondige
baraballa guNapadagaLu aSTondu sthiravalladiruva 'asthAyI'
guNadharma gaLannU sUcisuttave. vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa AkAra
(udda, ettara, teLu, agali, ityAdi), bhavtika mattu mAnasika
avasthegaLu (cikka, gaTTi, oNa, medu, kuruDu, jANa, ityAdi), baNNa
(kempu, biLI, kappu, ityAdi), prAya (hosa, hiri, ityAdi)
modalAdavu gaLannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLu nAmapadagaLondige
baruttave, mattu ghaTanegaLa vidhAna, samaya mattu jAgagaLannu
sUcisuva girane, sarane, taTakkane, mellane, mEle, munce, hinde
modalAda guNapadagaLu kriyApadagaLondige baruttave.

kannaDadalli I rIti mukhyavAgi eraDu rItiya guNapadagaLive
yAdarU sAmAnyavAgi guNapada (illavE 'guNavAcaka pada') embu
dannu I eraDu rItiya guNapadagaLannu oTTige sUcisuvudakkintalU
nAmapadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLannu mAtravE sUcisuvudakkAgi


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


baLasuvudu jAsti. mEle eraDaneya adhyAyadalli koTTiruva guNapada
gaLa guNadharmagaLalli ellavannU tOrisuvudu nAmapadagaLondige
baraballa guNapadagaLu mAtra. kriyApadagaLondige baraballa guNapada
gaLu avugaLalli kelavannu mAtra tOrisuttave.

udAharaNegAgi, nAmapadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLannu
nAmapadagaLinda bErpaDisi vAkyadallEnE bEre kaDegaLige vargAyisalu
sAdhyavAgadu. Adare kriyApadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLannu
vAkyadalli elli bEkiddarU baLasalu sAdhyavide. avu kriyApadada
hattiravE irabEkemba niyamavilla. udA:

1. (5ka) rAju maDikeyannu nelada mEle mellage irisida.
2. (5kha) rAju maDikeyannu mellage nelada mEle irisida.
3. (5ga) rAju maDikeyannu nelada mEle irisida, mellage.

mellage emba guNapada (maDikeyannu) irisiruvudu hEge embudAgi
irisuvike emba ondu ghaTaneya guNadharmavannu tiLisuttideyAdarU
adu (5ka)dalli mAtra A kriyApadada hattira bandide. (5kha)dalli adu
nelada embudarondigU mattu (5ga)dalli vAkyada horagU bandiru
vudannu kANabahudu.

kriyApadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLigiruva I svAtantryavannu
bEreyU kelavu viSayagaLalli kANabahudu. udAharaNegAgi, avakke
ottukoTTu, avannu vAkyadinda pratyEkisi hELalu sAdhyavide. Adare
nAmapadagaLondige baruva guNapadagaLannu I rIti pratyEkisi hELalu
sAdhyavAgadu.

(Ta) rAju maDikeyannu, nelada mEle mellage irisaballi.

(Tavi) rAju maDikeyannirisiddu mellage.

## 7.3 guNapadagaLa svarUpa
kannaDadalli oLaracaneyillada guNa(pada) dhAtugaLu halavive. ivugaLalli
ondE akSaraviruva dhAtugaLella asvatantra padagaLAgiddu, jODupada
gaLalli (nAmapadagaLAgi) illavE pratyayaviruva padagaLalli (guNapada
gaLAgi) baLakeyaguttave. udAharaNegAgi, kem emba asvatantra guNa
dhAtu kendALi, kemmaNNu modalAda jODupadagaLalli bEre pada


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


gaLondige sEri nAmapadavAgi baLakeyAguttade, mattu kempu mattu
kencu embavugaLalli pratyayagaLondige sEri guNapadavAgi baLake
yAguttade. hin, taN, mun, nuN, her (hiri) modalAdavugaLu
intaha ondakSaraviruva guNadhAtugaLu.

ondakkinta jAsti akSaraviruva guNadhAtugaLU kannaDadalli halavive.
cAritrikavAgi I dhAtugaLU ondakSara dhAtugaLige pratyayagaLannu sErisu
vudara mUlaka siddhavAdavugaLendu hELalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi,
biLi, bisi mattu kari embavugaLa koneya ikAra, sihi mattu kahi
embavugaLalli baruva hi emba eraDaneya akSara, eLe, haLe, oLLe
modalAdavugaLa koneyalli baruva ekAra, modalAdavugaLu I rIti
pratyayagaLAgiralu sAdhyavide.

kannaDadalli kriyAdhAtu mattu nAmadhAtugaLiginta binnavAgiruva
halavAru guNadhAtugaLiveyembudannu keLagina kelavu udAharaNegaLinda
tiLiyabahudu.

kelavu aNakisuva padagaLu I rIti ana emba pratyayada sahAya
villadeyU nEravAgi kriyApadagaLondige avugaLa viSESaNagaLAgi bara
balluvu. udAharaNegAgi, gaDagaDa naDugu, gusu gusu mAta
nADu, paLapaLa hoLe modalAda baLakegaLannu gamanisabahudu. ida
llade, endu emba padada sahAyadinda aNakisuva kelavu padagaLannu
etti hELalu sAdhyavide (udA: jO jO endu hADu). Adare
I eraDaneya vidhAnadalli baruva aNakisuva padagaLannu
guNapadagaLendu kareyuvudu kaSTa.

kelavu aNakisuva padagaLu ane emba pratyayada sahAyadinda
guNa padagaLAgiyU mattu isu emba pratyayada sahAyadinda
kriyApada gaLAgiyU baLakeyAgaballuvu (6.4 nODi). intaha
asvatantra dhAtu gaLu kriyAdhAtugaLE athavA guNadhAtugaLE
embudannu niSkxSTavAgi hELalu sAdhyavilla.

gamagamane gamagamisu
taLataLane taLataLisu
baDabaDane baDabaDisu
gahagahane gahagahisu

kannaDadalli baLakeyAguvantaha aNakisuva padagaLa akSara svarUpa
dalli kelavu vaySiSTyagaLive. avugaLallella modalige ondu vyanjana
bandiruttade. modalige svara bandiruva aNakisuva pada kannaDadalli
bahuSaH illavendE hELalU sAdhyavide. idallade, jODiyAgi baruva
padagaLalli (udA: kaTakaTane, caTacaTane, ityAdi) ottakSaravAgali,
udda svaravAgali kANisuvudilla, mattu I rIti jODiyAgi
bAradiruva padagaLalli (udA: barane, Dabbane, paTArane, kabakkane,
sarakkane, ityAdi) ottakSaravAgali, uddasvaravAgali kANisadiruvudilla.

## 7.4 pratyayagaLa baLake

© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


asvatantra guNadhAtugaLinda guNapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi kelavu
pratyayagaLu aniyamitavAgi baLakeyAguttave. kem-kempu, kari-kappu,
taN-tampu embavugaLalli kANisuva pu emba pratyaya intahadu.
Adare, hoLe-hoLapu, biLi-biLupu, mudi-muppu embavugaLalli
idE pratyaya guNapadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi
baLakeyAgide embu dannu gamanisabahudu.

kem-kencu embudaralli cu emba pratyaya baLakeyAgide, mattu
idE pratyaya mune-monacu embudaralli nAmapadadinda guNapada
vondannu tayArisalu baLakeyAgide. mum-munce embudaralli ce
emba innondu pratyaya baLakeyAgide, mattu idE pratyaya koLe-
koLace embudaralli kriyApadadinda guNapada (illavE
nAmapada)vannu tayArisalu baLakeyAgide. tumbu-tumba (tumbA),
agalu-agali embavugaLalli kriyApadadinda guNapadavannu tayArisalu
a (illavE A) emba pratyaya bandiruvudannu kANabahudu.

nAmapadagaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLinda kriyApadagaLondige
baraballa guNapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgiyU kelavu pratyayagaLa
baLakeyAguttade. ivugaLalli age embudE prAmukhyavAdudu. I
pratyayada baLakeyannu keLagina guNapadagaLalli kANabahudu.

I pratyayavannu sErisidAga guNapadadalli aniyamitavAgi bEre
bEre rItiya badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttave. udAharaNegAgi, biLi, bisi
mattu midu embavugaLa modalaneya akSaradalliruva ikAra ekAra
vAguttade. (nijakkU illi naDediruva cAritrika badalAvaNe idakke
viruddhavAdudu: pUrvada haLegannaDadalli I svara ellA kaDegaLallU
ekAravAgittu; Adare anantara biLi, bisi modalAdavugaLa eraDaneya


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


akSaradalli ikAra bandideyAda kAraNa adu ikAravAgittu, mattu
beccage, beLLage modalAda padagaLa eraDaneya akSaradalli ikArada
badalu akAravideyAda kAraNa, A ekAra badalAgade hAgeyE uLi
dittu.)

age emba pratyayavannoLagonDiruva bEreyU kelavu guNapada
gaLu kannaDadalliveyAdarU avakke nEravAgi bEre guNapadagaLondige
sambandhavannu sAdhisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla. udAharaNegAgi teppage
emba padavannu teravu emba nAmapadadondige hOlisidAga adaralli
I pratyayavideyendu anisuttade. I age emba pratyaya nAmapada
gaLondige baruva ge emba vibhakti pratyayakke sambandhiside embudannu
kone emba nAmapadadinda tayArAgiruva konege emba pada
sUcisu ttade.

nijakkU vibhakti pratyayagaLondige baruva nAmapadagaLigU mattu
kriyApadagaLondige baruva guNapadagaLigU naDuve hattirada sambandha
vide. vibhakti pratyayagaLu nAmapadagaLannu kriyApadagaLondige sambandhi
suttave mattu I kAraNakkAgi, avu ondu rItiyalli guNapadagaLa hAge
kriyApadagaLa viSESaNagaLAgiveyendU hELalu sAdhyavide.

## 7.5 sArAmSa
guNapadagaLa racaneyallU pratyayagaLa baLake jAstiyilla. nAmapada
gaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLinda kriyApadagaLondige baraballa guNa
padagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi mAtra, halavu padagaLalli kANisikoLLuva
age emba pratyaya baLakeyAguttade. idannu biTTare pratyayagaLa baLake
heccAgi kANisikoLLuvudu SabdagaLannu illavE anubhavagaLannu aNakisu
vantaha padagaLa baLakeyalli mAtra.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


<a id="adhyAya-8"></a><a id="eravalu-padagaLa-oLaracane"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-8) | [English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-8--internal-structure-of-loanwords)

## adhyAya enTueravalu padagaLa oLaracane

## 8.1 eraDaneya svarUpa
kannaDadalli samskxta, ingliS, hindi, parSiyan modalAda bEre
bEre bhASegaLinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLu halavive. ivugaLa
oLaracane hindina adhyAyagaLalli vivarisida kannaDa padagaLa oLaracaneginta
bhinna vAgiruvudAda kAraNa avannu pratyEkavAgi pariSIlisuva
avaSyakateyide. antaha pariSIlaneyannu I adhyAyadalli mADalAgide.
Adare kannaDadavE Ada padagaLu mattu bEre bhASegaLinda
eravalAgi banda padagaLu embudAgi kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva pada
gaLannu eraDu bEre bEre vargagaLalli vibhajisi hELuvudu mAtra
aSTondu sulabhada kelasavEnalla. yAkendare anAdi kAladindalU
intaha padagaLa eravalu namma bhASeyalli naDeyuttiddu, I
prakriyeya mUlaka adaralli sErikonDiruva padagaLalli bahaLa ittIcege
bandavugaLu mAtra tammatanavannu uLisikonDu bEre rItiya padagaLa
hAge kANisuttave. uLiduvella bEre bEre badalAvaNegaLa mUlaka
kannaDadavE AgibiTTive.

## 8.1.1 bhASegaLoLage eraDalinalli vayvidhya
ellA bhASegaLigU ondalla ondu vidhadalli bEre bhASegaLondige
samparkaviddE iruttadeyAda kAraNa, ellA bhASegaLallU eravalAgi
banda padagaLu iddE iruttave. kelavu bhASegaLalli intaha padagaLu
jAsti iruttave, mattu bEre kelavu bhASegaLalli kaDime iruttave

© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


embudE I viSayadalli bEre bEre bhASegaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa. I
vyatyAsakke halavu kAraNagaLive.

padagaLannu eravalu koDuva bhASegU mattu eravalu paDeyuva
bhASegU naDuve bahaLa hattirada samparkavideyAdare, mattu eravalu
koDuva bhASe heccu pratiSTheyadAdare, heccu heccu padagaLu adarinda
eralAgi bandu eravalu paDeyuva bhASeyalli sErikoLLalu sAdhyavide.
kannaDada maTTige samskxta bahaLa pratiSTheya bhASeyAgittAda kAraNa
adarinda doDDa sankhyeyalli padagaLu kannaDakke eravalAgi bandive.
ivattu ingliS bhASe antahadE pratiSTheya sthAnadallideyAda kAraNa
adarindalU padagaLu heccina sankhyeyalli eravalAgi baruttive.

idallade, ondu bhASeyannADuva janara manasthitiyantahadu,
avaru sulabhavAgi padagaLa eravalige marehoguvavarE athavA hosa
hosa padagaLannu baLasabEkAguva sandarbha bandAgalella tammavE Ada
padagaLannu sxSTisikoLLuvavarE embudu I vyatyAsakke innondu
AdhAravAguttade. tamma bhASeya kuritAgi jAsti abhimAnavannu
hondiruva mandi eravaligintalU hosa padagaLa tayArikegEnE kay
hAkuvudu jAsti.

bhASeyallillada hosa padagaLa avaSyakate bEre bEre kAraNagaLigAgi
kANisikoLLuttade. bErondu bhASeyannADuva janaralli baLakeyalliruva
vastugaLu nammalli baLakege bandAga, antaha vastugaLannu hesarisuvu
dakkAgi namage hosa padagaLa avaSyakate kanDubaruttade. intaha
sandarbhagaLalli A vastugaLondige avugaLa hesarugaLannU nAvu Amadu
mADikoLLabahudu, illavE nammavE Ada hesarugaLannu tayArisi
avakke koDabahudu.

udAharaNegAgi, ingliS bhASeyannADuva samAjadinda nAvu
rEDiyO, Ti.vi., bassu, kAru, pennu, raylu, kampyUTar modalAda
halavAru vastugaLannu baLakege paDediddu, avugaLondige A vastugaLa
hesarugaLannU eravalAgi paDedukonDiddEve. intaha vastugaLalli kela
vakke (udA: ugibanDi) nammavE Ada hesarugaLannu koTTiruvevAdarU
bEre kelavakke avugaLa hesarugaLannE alpa svalpa badalAvaNegaLondige
uLisikonDiddEve.

I rIti hosa hosa rItiya vastugaLannu baLakege paDedukoLLu
vudu mAtravalla, hosa hosa viSayagaLannU nAvu bEre bhASegaLa
nnADuva janarinda tiLidukoLLuvavAddarinda antaha viSayagaLannu


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


hesarisuva padagaLU namma bhASege eravalAgi baruttave. I rItiyalli
eravAlAgi bandiruva nUrAru padagaLannu SAstrIya granthagaLalli kANa
bahudu. namma dinanityada baLakeyalliruva bhASeyallU intaha hala
vAru padagaLu bEre bhASegaLinda eravalAgi bandu sErikonDiruttave.

## A.1.2 tattva mattu tadbhava padagaLu
I rIti eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli samskxta bhASeyinda bandavu
gaLannu mAtra avugaLa svarUpavannAdharisi tadbhava mattu tadbhava
embudAgi vingaDisi hELuva krama kannaDada vyAkaraNagaLalli mattu
arthakOSagaLalli baLakeyallide. samskxtadalli iruva hAgeyE baLake
yAguva padagaLu (endare samskxtada padagaLige samAnavAda padagaLu)
tadbhavagaLu mattu antaha padagaLalli bEre bEre rItiya badalAvaNe
gaLAdudarindAgi avugaLiginta bhinnavAgiruva padagaLu tadbhavagaLu
(endare samskxtadinda janisida padagaLu) embudAgi I vibhajaneyannu
varNisabahudu. Adare, sAmAnyavAgi padagaLa koneya bhAgadalli
mAtravE badalAvaNeyAgideyAdare, antaha padagaLannu tadbhavagaLendu
hELade tadbhavagaLendu hELuvudE rUDhi (SrIkanThayya 1952:196
nODi).

udAharaNegAgi, yAva badalAvaNeyannU tOrisadiruva satya,
dharma, adhikAri, kapi modalAdavugaLannu mattu koneyalli mAtravE
badalAvaNeyannu tOrisuva SAle (SAlA), janani (jananI),
manassu (manas) modalAdavugaLannu tatsama padagaLendU mattu
itara bhAgagaLalli badalAvaNegaLannu tOrisuva Ase (ASA), nidde
(nidrA), huNNime (pUrNimA), batti (varti) modalAda padagaLannu
tadbhava padagaLendU kareyuva krama rUDhiyallide.

intaha padagaLa vibhajane inDO-Aryan emba bhASAkuTumbakke
sEriruva prAkxta, pAli, hindi, marAThi, gujarAti modalAda bhASegaLa
vyAkaraNa mattu arthakOSagaLa maTTige bahaLa upayuktavAdudendu
hELalu sAdhyavide. nijakkU I bhASegaLalli tatsama mattu tadbhava emba
eraDu rItiya padagaLu mAtra ive. ivugaLalli tadbhava padagaLella
cAritrikavAgi samskxtakkU mattu avakkU oTTige mUla bhASeyA
giruva inDO-Aryan‌ninda beLedubandavugaLu. samskxtada padagaLi
ginta bhinnavAgilladiruva tatsama padagaLu mAtra nEravAgi samskxtadinda
eravalAgi bandavugaLu embudAgi parigaNisalu sAdhyavide.


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


Adare kannaDa bhASe idakkinta tIra bhinnavAgiruva drAviDa bhASA
kuTumbakke sEriruva kAraNa, adaralli tatsama mattu tadbhava padagaLu
mAtravallade mUla bhASeyinda beLedu bandiruva drAviDa padagaLU
halavive. nijakkU kannaDadalli kANisuva tatsama mattu tadbhava
padagaLeraDU samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLE. avugaLa
naDuviruva vyatyAsavEnendare, tatsama padagaLalli kaDime badalAvaNegaLu
naDedive mattu tadbhava padagaLalli jAsti badalAvaNegaLu naDedive.
hAgAgi, kannaDada vyAkaraNa illavE arthakOSada maTTige tatsama-
tadbhavavemba eravalu padagaLa vibhajaneyinda viSiSTavAda prayOjana
vEnU illa. kannaDada maTTige samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLa
nnella ondE vibhAgadalli irisi pariSIlisidare sAkAguttade.

## A.1.3 badalAvaNegaLige kAraNagaLu
eravalAgi banda padagaLu bEre bEre kAraNagaLigAgi badalAvaNegaLige
oLagAguttave. avannu eravalAgi koTTa bhASegU mattu eravalAgi
paDedukonDa bhASegU naDuve varNagaLa sankhyeya maTTige mattu
varNagaLu padagaLalli baruva kramada maTTige vyatyAsagaLiveyAdare,
padagaLannu eravalAgi paDeyuva bhASe tanna varNavyavasthege hondi
koLLuvante avugaLalli badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLuttade. udAharaNe
gAgi kannaDadalli mahAprANAkSaragaLu mUlataH iralillavAdudarinda,
samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda halavAru padagaLalli mahAprANakSaragaLu
alpaprANAkSaragaLAgi badalAgive. udA: bIdi (vIthi), sante
(samsthA), dAre (dhArA), bandi (bandhi), ityAdi.

innondu bhASeyinda jAsti padagaLannu eravalu paDediruva bhASe
avugaLondige kelavu hosa varNagaLannU paDedukonDiralu sAdhyavide,
mattu anantara A bhASeyinda eravalAgi baruva padagaLalli antaha
varNagaLu badalAgade uLiyalu sAdhyavide. kannaDada kelavu prabhEda
gaLalli (udA: barahada kannaDa) I rIti heccu heccu mahA
prANAkSaragaLiruva padagaLu eravalAgi bandudarindAgi antaha akSara
gaLu A prabhEdada varNagaLAgibiTTive. tatsama mattu tadbhavagaLemba
eraDu rItiya eravalAda padagaLu kannaDadalli kANisalu idU ondu
kAraNa. tadbhavagaLu badalAvaNe avaSyavendu kANisuva samayadalli
banda padagaLu, mattu tatsamagaLu A avaSyakate illavAdAga eravalAgi
banda padagaLu. Adare I rItiya vayvidhyate ingliS, hindi


© DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.


modalAda bhASegaLinda kannaDakke eravalAgi banda padagaLallU
kANisuttade.

bhASeya varNagaLalli mattu avugaLa vyavastheyalli kAladinda kAlakke
badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttA iruttave. I badalAvaNegaLu A
bhASeyavE Agiruva padagaLalli mAtravallade, A bhASege bEre bhASe
gaLinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLallU naDeyuttave. eravalAgi
bandiruva padagaLalli kANisuva halavu vyatyAsagaLige intaha cAritrika
badalAvaNe innondu mukhya kAraNa.

udAharaNegAgi, kannaDadalli sumAru ondu sAvira varSagaLaSTu
hinde padagaLa Adiyalli baruva pakAra hakAravAguva badalAvaNe
yondu naDeyitu. I badalAvaNeya phalavannu kannaDadavE Ada
padagaLalli mAtravallade, samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva pada
gaLallU kANabahudu.

1. (1) kannaDada padagaLalli pakAra hakAravAgiruvudu
2. haLegannaDa hosagannaDa
3. pAl hAlu
4. paN haNNu
5. puli huli
6. pO hO(gu)
8. (2) samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLalli pakAra hakAra
9. vAgiruvudu
10. samskxta kannaDa
11. pakSi hakki
12. paSu hasu
13. parva habba
14. piSTa hiTTu

idE rItiyalli giDDasvarada anantara baruva rakAravu, adara
anantara vyanjanavondu bandiddAga, A vyanjanadondige sEri ottakSara
vAguva badalAvaNe kannaDadavE Ada padagaLalli mAtravallade samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLallU naDedide.
